General Committee Meeting Yesterday: Disarmament Reaches a Critical Juncture; Discord Between Britain and France Cannot Be Resolved; Meeting Adjourned to Next Tuesday

Delegate Gu Expresses Deep Concern That Failure of Disarmament Will Affect the Far East

Advocates Collective System to Guarantee Security

Simon Leaves Geneva to Return to London

(Geneva) At the General Committee meeting of the Disarmament Conference this afternoon, Chairman Henderson lamented the seriousness of the current situation and urged all delegates to continue negotiations and establish an arms convention. He then proposed that the General Committee meeting be postponed to next Tuesday, so that the delegates could reflect on the very critical situation that has arisen and so that the British and French delegates could resolve their differences and reach a compromise. Before the General Committee meeting began, the atmosphere in the lounge was tense. Delegates gathered in groups of three or five, discussing the future of the Disarmament Conference, speaking freely and without concealment. Everyone felt that the Disarmament Conference had reached a critical juncture. At 3:45 PM, Henderson solemnly ascended the podium and announced the opening of the meeting, fifteen minutes later than scheduled. After Henderson urged the delegates to save the Disarmament Conference with solemn words, he read out the resolution passed by the League of Nations Cooperation Committee at Folkestone, which emphatically stated that if the Disarmament Conference failed, the situation would be unimaginably dangerous. The delegates were surprised to learn that British Foreign Secretary Simon had purchased a night train ticket and was preparing to return to London immediately. People held different views on this matter, some saying that Simon's return was to consult with the cabinet, while others said that Simon felt that staying in Geneva for a long time would not help the overall situation, so he returned to London. (Reuters dispatch on the 1st)

(Geneva) At the meeting of the Disarmament General Committee, Chairman Henderson said in his speech that the current situation of the Disarmament Conference is extremely serious, more so than at any time. He is very anxious. The current situation cannot be resolved merely by expressing opinions. Therefore, he proposed to postpone the meeting to next Tuesday and hold a main body meeting on Monday, so that the delegates would have ample opportunity to consider the matter at the end of this week. By then, the delegates may be able to find a way to proceed. Everyone wants complete success, without a doubt, but a concession must be obtained and put into practice.

Poland Rejects Russian Proposal for Security Organization, Sides Against France

Polish Foreign Minister Beck criticized the plan for a permanent body proposed by Russian Foreign Minister Litvinov, pointing out that it conflicts with the authority of the League of Nations. Apart from that, he is willing to support any proposal that can solve this problem.

Mr. Gu Weijun's Speech: Security and Disarmament Are Inseparable

Chinese Envoy to France, Dr. Gu Weijun, took the floor and said that since the opening of the Disarmament Conference, the Chinese delegation has focused on finding a satisfactory solution to the security issue, as this issue is the real cause of various difficulties. Dr. Gu went on to say that we have expressed more than once the opinion that if the existing collective action system is not implemented, the disarmament cause will be in danger. If the international treaty stipulating the peaceful resolution of international disputes and prohibiting the use of force as a policy tool is despised and undermined without being prevented by collective action, then no one will be willing to engage in disarmament rashly. Gentlemen, you still remember that when the Disarmament Conference had just opened its doors and started working, an undeclared war broke out in the Far East. One country, with its superior army, invaded another country, completely disregarding the solemn obligations under international treaties. This international treaty is regarded by the world as the most important support for peace. However, for two and a half years, what the aggressor has gained remains with the aggressor, and not a single person has helped the victim. Even the common obligations under the League of Nations Covenant are ineffective. This undeniable fact and lesson cannot be forgotten by farsighted politicians. In short, the current collective peace system has not achieved sufficient security at all. Security is a fundamental issue and cannot be separated from the disarmament issue. If there is a general agreement to formulate an effective security system based on collective guarantees and ensure its effective implementation, then the disputes over other aspects of the disarmament issue will be easily resolved. He expressed his agreement with the British Foreign Secretary Simon's statement that the security issue is a matter of degree, not a matter of principle. If armaments cannot be completely abolished, then merely reducing armaments without supplementing them with a security system based on collective guarantees and compulsory implementation will ultimately fail to secure peace. (Reuters dispatch on the 1st)

(Geneva) The talks and mediation of third parties have not yet melted the differences between Britain and France. French Foreign Minister Barthou received a telegram from French Prime Minister Doumergue, praising his amazing speech on Wednesday, so the French side's attitude became more and more firm. The general feeling is that if there is no unexpected development, the only method that can be adopted when the Disarmament General Committee meets at 3:30 this afternoon is to announce an adjournment, pending an understanding between the major powers. Without this understanding, negotiations will never succeed. However, the representatives of small countries may make a final effort to advocate the discussion of the three points proposed by British Foreign Secretary Simon, namely: 1) Limiting chemical warfare; 2) Publicizing the budget; 3) Establishing a permanent disarmament committee. France has always opposed the publicity of the budget, unless the publicity of the budget and the restriction of the budget are carried out at the same time. In any case, it is recognized that this method is insignificant compared to the original grand plan of the Disarmament Conference. (Reuters dispatch on the 1st)

(Geneva) The survival of the Disarmament Conference will be decided tomorrow. Although the general opinion is that the postponement of the Disarmament Conference is the only solution, the current atmosphere is extremely uneasy. Chairman Henderson told a Reuters reporter tonight that in the past two and a half years, the situation has been more serious than it is today. If it does not change quickly, there is no hope for the situation. The representatives are extremely unwilling to clearly state their positions. The discussion may end at the General Committee meeting tomorrow. The representatives of Spain and Sweden are now working hard to reconcile the attitudes of Britain and France, and will re-submit the Swedish memorandum of April 14, which has been approved by the Netherlands, Denmark, Norway, Spain, and Switzerland, with slight revisions. The memorandum advocates: 1) Immediately find a way to prevent the existing situation from deteriorating; 2) Unconditionally prohibit aerial bombardment; 3) Truly reduce armaments; 4) Give adequate but practical realization to the principle of equal rights. (Reuters dispatch on the 30th)

(Geneva) Since British Foreign Secretary Simon and French Foreign Minister Barthou made their speeches and argued with each other yesterday, the League of Nations has been in chaos. Seeing this, the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, specially devised a way to postpone the meeting to Friday so that the delegations of various countries would have more time to consider the opportunity. Now, all parties in Geneva feel that the differences between Britain and France have deepened to the point of being irreconcilable, and the death of the Disarmament Conference is imminent. However, in order to prevent the interruption of the conference discussion, some people have suggested to the Soviet Russian Foreign Commissar Litvinov to submit a proposal to the Disarmament Conference, which contains the main points of his speech the other day. This may be the life-saving soup of the Disarmament Conference, which is not necessarily true. Furthermore, British Foreign Secretary Simon will submit a proposal for the organization of a permanent disarmament conference at the next meeting, which may also be put to discussion. Furthermore, the differences between the matters proposed by Simon and Litvinov are also very obvious, that is, the main point advocated by Litvinov is "security," while Simon's advocacy is still to disarm. (National Telegram on the 30th)

Only Seeking to End the Meeting, Britain Has No Extravagant Hopes; It Is Okay to Narrow the Scope and Conclude a Convention; Organize Security by the Concentric Circle Method

(London) The majority party in Parliament openly hopes that the disarmament issue can be resolved, but the diplomatic community believes that ending the Disarmament Conference is not appropriate at least at the moment, so it continues to hope that a disarmament convention can be concluded within the scope of the following four points: 1) Limiting the air force; 2) Prohibiting chemical and germ warfare; 3) Supervising armaments; 4) Organizing security by the "concentric circle" method. However, Britain's participation in the organization is limited to mutual consultation (according to concentric circles, or the so-called regional treaties concluded by various countries to guarantee security, each region is a concentric circle). In order to deal with the Labor Party, which is the opposition party, the government party clearly wants to cover up the failure of disarmament, and it is really necessary to cover it up. Therefore, even Litvinov's claim is to be reviewed and the part that can be considered by the United Kingdom is taken. Within a certain range, the Italian plan is also intended to be adopted, as long as France agrees. However, British people do not have extravagant hopes for the success of disarmament. Therefore, even if the scope is very small, if international consensus can be obtained, the United Kingdom will be happy to accept it, as if relieved of a heavy burden, so as to prove that the efforts to prevent war are not completely ineffective. (Havas dispatch on the 30th)

(London) Although the British side has not responded to the Soviet Union's Foreign Minister Litvinov's proposal to the Disarmament General Committee, most British public opinion hopes that the Disarmament Conference will prolong its life due to Litvinov's proposed European security pact. This is difficult to deny. For example, the Liberal Party's organ newspaper "Manchester Guardian" has this attitude. The newspaper said that Litvinov only made a verbal proposal and has not yet submitted a specific draft resolution, but some small countries see that the Disarmament Conference has not achieved anything so far, so it is better to have this resolution than nothing, and it may be submitted as soon as possible. In any case, if any disarmament convention seeks to have a little value, then the security issue must not be ignored. We should participate in the solution of the security issue, but we cannot prove that the United Kingdom has clearly understood the method of solving the security issue. If small countries and the Soviet Union do propose a formal proposal for a European security pact, then in any case, before the Disarmament Conference admits defeat, it is necessary to review this proposal. League of Nations Discusses Chaco Dispute: Resolution to Handle It in Accordance with Article Fifteen of the Covenant; Arms Embargo Only Luxembourg Has Not Replied

(Geneva) The Council of the League of Nations decided today to handle the dispute between Paraguay and Bolivia over the Chaco in accordance with Article Fifteen of the League Covenant at the request of the Bolivian government. Although Germany has not formally replied, it has indicated that it is willing to abide by any resolution of the Council on this matter. According to Article Fifteen of the Covenant, the dispute will be submitted to the Council, and the Council will try its best to resolve it. Otherwise, the Council will publish the facts of the dispute and its recommendations, which it considers fair and appropriate. Now Paraguay has agreed to submit this dispute to the Council, so the Chaco War, which has been going on for a long time, may be resolved peacefully. (Reuters dispatch on the 1st)

Moreover, Paraguay can navigate unimpeded, while Bolivia has been surrounded. (National Telegram on the 30th)

A Grand Spectacle of Roosevelt's Grand Review of the American Navy and Air Force

Report on the Expected Withdrawal of the Manila Fleet and Arrest of Japanese Espionage

(London) The Morning Post's diplomatic correspondent reported news that the United States intends to withdraw its fleet stationed in Manila. It is said that according to the Philippine Independence Act, the United States can maintain a naval base in the Philippine Islands. The reason for this move, it is understood, is strategic. Because the fleet is too weak, it cannot withstand possible enemy attacks before reinforcements arrive. The move by the United States to maintain a naval base in Manila may make it easier to establish a US-Japan treaty, but what will happen to Hong Kong, Singapore, etc.? There is no answer here yet. Furthermore, Britain and Japan may also be able to conclude a treaty regarding these places. (1st, Reuters)

(New York) The largest naval assembly and maneuver in American history is now coming to an end. This morning, ninety-six warships sailed back from the sea and up the Hudson River, passing the cruiser Indianapolis, aboard which President Roosevelt was sailing. A grand review will be held by President Roosevelt, the Commander-in-Chief, this afternoon. The US Navy began its third annual test of US naval power efficiency on May 5th. The voyage was six thousand miles, and the maneuver location was in the Caribbean Sea, starting from the Panama Canal to the Virgin Islands. Two weeks after the maneuver, the warships went to Guantanamo Bay and then to New York to participate in the grand review. The feature of this year's exercise was the defense of the Panama Canal. All actions were as if in wartime. News from the Panama Canal was strictly checked. When the fleet passed through the canal, many merchant ships were not allowed to enter or exit, which lasted about twenty-four hours. (31st, Reuters)

(New York) President Roosevelt, aboard the flagship Indianapolis, reviewed the American fleet advancing up the Hudson River today. Naval aircraft soared over the entrance to New York Harbor. The fleet proceeded like a long snake, led by huge battleships, followed by agile destroyers, and submarines bringing up the rear. It was a rare spectacle of sea and air power not seen in peacetime. Millions of spectators were on the riverbanks and yachts. The USS Pennsylvania led the line, firing a 21-gun salute as it passed the President's flagship. Sailors and officers on board were in full dress uniform, saluting with their rifles. Each ship was freshly painted, spotless, and gleaming under the morning sun, like jewels. Fighter planes from the aircraft carriers took off one by one, performing various flying techniques, first flying in formation, then demonstrating bombing, smoke screens, and other wartime maneuvers. There was heavy fog on the Hudson River at first, which delayed the start of the review slightly, but the fog soon cleared, and the sun shone again. After passing the flagship, the fleet entered New York Bay and anchored. Officers and sailors were free to go ashore. Accompanying the President on the flagship were the Chief of Naval Operations, Standley, the Assistant Secretary of the Navy, Henry Roosevelt, and news reporters aboard the heavy cruiser USS Louisville. (31st, National Telegram)

(New York) Forty thousand sailors participating in President Roosevelt's naval review arrived here last night. Residents were excited and came out to welcome them. When the sailors landed, the piers were full of their sweethearts, families, and onlookers. President Roosevelt's face was slightly tanned by the sun. When he disembarked, he had a beaming smile. The cheers of the crowd were deafening. The President then departed for Groton, Massachusetts. Although there was fog at the beginning of the review, it soon cleared, and the military appearance was extremely impressive. Crowds gathered on the tops of tall buildings and the decks of ships, watching from afar. The whole city was in a naval mood that day, and many shops displayed women's sailor suits, etc. (1st, Havas)

(New York) Two Japanese men were arrested today for attempting to obtain secret information about the US Navy. The matter is currently under investigation. It is said that the two first tried to lure a retired sailor named Salowski with alcohol, and then inquired about the activities of the US fleet, especially the maneuvers in the Panama area and the Caribbean Sea. The two were later released on bail of $250. (31st, National News Agency)

Rumor of Assassination Attempt Against Roosevelt

(New York) Rumors spread that someone was plotting to throw a bomb at President Roosevelt's special train, so the police authorities have taken special precautions. A special guard of twenty-five men accompanied the President's special train for protection, and another seventy guards, fully armed, were stationed around the station. Undercover agents were also deployed everywhere. When the special train arrived, no one without a pass was allowed into the station. There are no leads on the plotters, but since Roosevelt was elected President, there have been several attempts to harm him, so this rumor must be given special attention. (31st, National Telegram)

Sino-Italian Friendship: Chinese Envoy Hosts Mussolini; Chinese Inspection Delegation Assembles in Rome

(Rome) Italian Prime Minister Mussolini was hosted at the Chinese Embassy for the first time tonight. The Prime Minister wore the First Class Precious Jade Medal awarded by the Chinese government in March of this year. The Chinese Envoy and his staff were deeply impressed by Mussolini's respect for etiquette. During the dinner, Liu Wendao said in his speech, "We Chinese all consider Your Excellency to be the greatest figure in centuries." Mussolini then gave a reply, praising China's two thousand years of culture. The inspection delegation led by Yu Feipeng, Vice Minister of Communications, will arrive here on Sunday. Italian circles are paying close attention. Yu's trip is to inspect the Italian railway, postal, and wireless telegraph systems. Xu Tingyao and others are also traveling with him. In addition, the Chinese Kuomintang delegation inspecting the Fascist system has also arrived here. All of this can be regarded as evidence of the deep friendship between China and Italy. The delegation will go to Germany within days to inspect the National Socialist Party's system. (1st, Reuters)

Italy Does Not Consider Japan's Declaration of Blockading China to Be Concluded; Still Skeptical of Hirota's Assurances

(Rome) Today, it was expressed here that Italy does not consider Japan's declaration of blockading China to be concluded. Italian newspapers today published in their conspicuously suggested articles that the Italian Ambassador to Japan, Auriti, is now questioning the Japanese government, asking it to explain the statement made by the Foreign Ministry spokesman on April 17th. Italy has taken note of Foreign Minister Hirota's assurance that Japan is determined to respect existing treaties, but Italy must still make it clear that a policy of hegemony over China is ultimately dangerous. Italy's attitude towards China is based on humanitarianism and believes that this policy is beneficial to China and world peace. The United Kingdom and the United States responded to Japan's declaration the earliest, but Italy has not yet made an official statement. (1st, National Telegram)

Wireless Communication Between Japan and Italy

(Osaka) The Nagoya Wireless Station and the Rome Wireless Station exchanged official documents via telegraph at 9:00 AM today. This is the first direct wireless communication between Japan and Italy. (1st, China United Press)

Another German Pocket Battleship; Completion Expected by the End of This Month; No Refueling Needed En Route; Can Sail Directly to the Far East at High Speed

(Berlin) According to news today, Germany's third pocket battleship will be launched on June 30th. This ship, like the previous two, has a displacement of 10,000 tons and is equipped with 11-inch guns. At a speed of 20 knots, it can travel 10,000 miles. It is said that it can reach the Far East directly without refueling en route. Its 11-inch guns fire 670-pound shells and can reach 30,000 yards at a 60-degree elevation. Its engine is a diesel type, especially lightweight. In addition to six 11-inch guns, it is also equipped with eight 6-inch guns, eight small guns, and four torpedo tubes. (1st, Reuters)

German Industrial and Financial Circles Form New Organization; Aim to Promote Economic Relations with the Far East

(Berlin) An organization called the German-East Association has recently been established here with official support. The association aims to promote economic and social relations between Germany and the East. All sectors related to Germany's Eastern trade have joined. The board of directors is composed of representatives from major industrial and commercial enterprises and banks. The chairman is Mr. Reiss, a director of Siemens. (1st, Reuters)

Opium Advisory Committee Discusses the Issue of Licenses in Manchukuo; Uses Lack of Qualification for Judgment as an Excuse; Japanese Representative Yokoyama Speaks Nonsense; Hu Shih-Tze Refutes with Strong Words

(Geneva) The Opium Advisory Committee held a closed meeting today to discuss the issue of opium import licenses in "Manchukuo." To avoid political disputes, most committee members advocated maintaining the current system, with consuls still issuing licenses. British representative Danafin insisted that these licenses did not have the same guarantees as import licenses. The committee then resolved that it was not qualified to judge who should issue import licenses. This matter should be mentioned in the report to the League of Nations Council. Japanese representative Yokoyama claimed that the opium situation in "Manchukuo" was left over from previous rulers, but he recently received a letter from a Japanese friend informing him that "Manchukuo" will continue to improve. Chinese representative Hu Shih-Tze then asked Yokoyama who his friend was, as Yokoyama had previously said that Japan had nothing to do with "Manchukuo." Yokoyama replied that they were consultants. Hu retorted that if they could handle opium issues, their status must be higher than consultants. The committee has adopted the report of the seizure subcommittee. The US representative to the Opium Conference, Fowler, also serves as the reporter for the seizure of secret drug manufacturing in China. It is said that most of the drugs seized were on ships sailing from Dalian to China. According to seizures in China and Hong Kong, China currently has a large number of secret manufacturing of morphine and heroin, mostly from Sichuan, Shanghai, and Peiping, followed by Shenyang and Harbin. The committee believes that the scope of secret drug manufacturing has expanded, which is not only a great harm to China but will also affect other parts of the world. (31st, Reuters)

Saar Plebiscite Issue; Three-Person Committee Drafts Plan; Stolen Documents Found in River

(Geneva) After several hours of discussion late last night, the representatives of France, Germany, and Italy finally drafted a plan for the Saar region's self-determination issue. This new method has been telegraphed to the governments concerned and is expected to receive a reply tonight. (1st, National News Agency)

(Paris) A boatman in the Saar region saw three packages floating in the water this morning at the border between the French and Saar regions of the Saar River. They were immediately salvaged, and what was inside was part of the documents stolen from the Education Bureau of the French state-owned coal mine area on the evening of the 22nd of this month. The Saar region authorities were immediately notified to conduct an investigation. The French authorities on the opposite bank assisted in the search and found four packages in the French part of the Saar River. It is estimated that they were thrown into the water not long ago. According to general speculation, all the stolen documents must be in the packages. (31st, Havas)

US Senate Approves New Treaty with Cuba

(Washington) The Senate today approved a new treaty between the United States and Cuba to replace the treaty of May 22, 1903. However, this new treaty still allows the United States to interfere in Cuban affairs to protect the lives and property of American citizens and allows the United States to militarily occupy Cuba and all measures taken during the time until the Cuban Republic is established to be perpetuated forever. The stipulation that the US Navy may establish a base in Guantanamo also remains in effect. This new treaty will take effect after both parties sign it. (31st, Reuters)

US House Passes Silver Bill; All Amendments Rejected; No Problem Expected in the Senate

(Washington) The House of Representatives today passed the Silver Bill by a large majority of 266 votes to 77. Before the bill was passed, the House rejected a motion to refer the bill to a committee to draft an amendment to issue silver certificates to purchase silver by a vote of 268 to 70. The bill was passed without any amendments. The government leaders were able to pass the bill without violating the President's wishes, and the government-appointed members were also able to reject all amendments proposed by the opposition party. The bill has now been sent to the Senate and will be debated soon. There will be some resistance to this bill in the Senate, but it will not have any significant impact. When the House passed the Silver Bill, the New York Merchants Association was also discussing the bill in New York and resolved to oppose it. (31st, National Telegram)

(Washington) The House of Representatives today passed the silver bill proposed by the silver faction members of the Senate by a vote of 263 to 77. This bill (1) stipulates increasing the amount of silver held by the United States and allows the President to receive silver currency from the public; (2) authorizes the Secretary of the Treasury to purchase silver at home and abroad in the market at prices, times, and conditions that he deems appropriate and most beneficial to the public. The purchase of silver domestically is limited to 50 cents per ounce of all silver on May 1st. The Secretary of the Treasury may also sell silver when the market price of silver exceeds the value of the currency, or when the amount of currency held exceeds the ratio of 75 gold to 25 silver; (3) the Secretary of the Treasury may issue silver certificates, the face value of which shall not be less than the cost of the silver purchased. In addition, the Secretary of the Treasury will regulate, investigate, and prohibit the purchase, import, and transportation of silver, and impose a fine of $10,000 or ten years in prison on all violators. The Secretary of the Treasury has the power to issue regulations that he deems appropriate to implement the purpose of this bill. At today's meeting, Democratic silver faction members opposed this bill, pointing out that this bill is equivalent to silver bricks and will prolong the depression for ten years. Republican members criticized this bill, believing that it lacks stability in currency. Democratic supporters of this bill said that the government's gold policy needs to be supplemented to increase prices and foreign trade. (31st, Reuters)

US Drought and Labor Strikes

(New York) Thirty-five states in the United States, from the Rocky Mountains to New England, are in a serious situation due to a prolonged drought. The rainfall in Iowa, Nebraska, Illinois, Indiana, and Ohio is particularly low, the lowest ever recorded. Even if these five states receive heavy rain within half a month, the harvest will only be half of normal. There are ten other states with similar situations. The temperature is extremely high in several places, exacerbating the disaster. The temperature in the shade in Aberdeen, South Dakota, reached 100 degrees Fahrenheit today, but the temperature in Minneapolis, Minnesota, was even higher, reaching 106 degrees. Iowa City also reached 105 degrees, and Chicago reached 102 degrees. Crops and livestock in the western states are showing signs of damage, and the International Wheat Agreement is also uncertain, so the government's restriction policy may change. Farmers in the disaster area are no longer bound by the restriction policy. Undersecretary of Agriculture Tugwell stated that the government may adopt a policy of expanding agricultural production rather than restricting it after considering the disaster. The increase in temperature and the fear of crop failure caused the price of wheat futures on the Chicago Board of Trade to soar today, reaching about one US dollar per bushel, the highest price since last fall. The official weather bureau predicts that the drought is unlikely to ease in the short term. Congress will inevitably face the issue of appropriating funds for disaster relief. As for how much money is needed, it is not yet possible to estimate. According to news today, the temperature in the shade in Elwood, Iowa, reached 111 degrees. The wheat that has not been destroyed is maturing very quickly. Farmers in Oklahoma and Kansas are currently engaged in harvesting. According to statisticians' estimates, one-third of the wheat in Iowa has not germinated in the soil. The central and state governments have now announced relief plans. According to Canadian telecommunications, several places in Canada are also suffering from drought, but the situation is gradually improving, and the heatwave has subsided. However, this year's wheat harvest is feared to be the smallest in sixteen years. (1st, Reuters)

(Washington) Since General Johnson, Director of the Reconstruction Administration, announced that the working hours of the textile industry would be reduced by a quarter to maintain the continued operation of textile factories during the summer, the labor unions have strongly opposed it. Three hundred thousand workers have been brewing a major strike. Reconstruction Administration personnel will meet with labor union leaders tomorrow to discuss ways to avoid a labor strike. (31st, National Telegram)

Toledo The electrical workers' strike here has been postponed until tomorrow to allow for negotiations with employers tonight to find a solution. Negotiations between the power plant and the labor union today were still fruitless. However, the situation is still calm, and the security forces are prepared to withdraw. (31st, National Telegram)

Baltimore The mediation plan proposed by the shipping industry here was rejected by the dockworkers' union today. The union received a telegram from its president, Ryan, which led to this decision. The telegram stated that during the strike, all shipyard workers along the East Coast would also boycott ships on the West Coast. (31st, National Telegram)

(Washington) People here today believe that the only way to avoid a national strike is for President Roosevelt to personally convene negotiations between labor and management after returning to the White House from New York. Some government officials also support this proposal. The steelworkers' union also hopes that the President will intervene. General Johnson, Director of the Reconstruction Administration, will convene a joint meeting of labor and management tomorrow to obtain more concrete results. (31st, National Telegram)

Romanian Minister of the Army Resigns

Capital of Romania Army Minister Uijia submitted his resignation, which has been approved by the King. General Uijia has been reassigned as the commander of the capital garrison. His vacant position as Minister of the Army will be temporarily held by Prime Minister Tatarescu. (1st, Havas)

Hejaz-Yemen War May Be Avoided; Yemen Accepts New Conciliation Terms

Cairo The fear of a resumption of hostilities between Hejaz and Yemen has been averted. According to news from Taif, the Yemeni Imam has changed his attitude and accepted the new conciliation terms of Hejaz King Ibn Saud. According to news from Sanaa, the Crown Prince of Yemen has also dispelled his opposition to his father signing the treaty. It is heard that one of the new terms is that Yemen leases Hodeidah, which is occupied by Hejaz, as a trading place and pays taxes to Hejaz. The content of the new terms has not yet been announced. It is believed that the terms proposed have been greatly revised. (31st, Reuters)

Sakano's Imprudent Remarks Lead to Dismissal, Uganda's Cabinet Formation Hope Dashed

(Tokyo) Amidst reports that the army and navy were absolutely opposed to Governor-General Ugaki forming a cabinet, Military Affairs Promotion Department Committee Chairman Sakano issued a statement yesterday endorsing Governor-General Ugaki of Korea's formation of a cabinet, causing considerable turmoil in political circles. At the same time, the navy, due to the passing of elder statesman Admiral Togo, felt an even greater need for unity. If that statement was issued in a way that seemed to represent the navy, there would be great regret over military control. People also regard the admiral's statement as naval interference in politics, and this has been highlighted. The anti-Ugaki faction within the army, seeing this situation, quickly gathered last night to oppose attacks on the navy. The navy also regarded the situation as serious and dismissed Committee Chairman Sakano, who had only been in office for three weeks. Therefore, the atmosphere aroused by the statement within the navy can be calmed down. Moreover, Major General Sakano and Governor-General Ugaki are both from Okayama, which made his position even more unfavorable. On the other hand, Governor-General Ugaki's entry into the political world will become even more difficult as a result of this. (1st, Electric News Agency)

(Tokyo) Navy Military Affairs Promotion Department Committee Chairman Major General Sakano's statement yesterday that "the military does not oppose the emergence of the Ugaki cabinet" was made in violation of the intentions of the navy's top brass. As a result, Major General Sakano incurred the wrath of the top brass and was dismissed from his position as Committee Chairman of the Military Affairs Promotion Department. (1st, Electric News Agency)

(Tokyo) Regarding the navy's statement that it would not obstruct the emergence of the Ugaki cabinet, the Seiyukai (political party) observes the following: The navy's statement indicates that it does not oppose the Ugaki cabinet, and at the same time, it will not take any action against the emergence of a party cabinet. This move may yield extremely good results for the emergence of a party cabinet that the majority of the people yearn for. (1st, Electric News Agency)

(Tokyo) The House of Peers' view on the Sakano issue is as follows: The content of Major General Sakano's statement this time is the same as the previous Amahisa statement, with little accurate understanding of the situation within the department. Therefore, its publication without the understanding of the superior, from the point of view of maintaining military discipline, can be said to be inattentive. From this, it can be seen that the atmosphere within the navy opposing Ugaki's appointment to the cabinet is relatively strong. (1st, Electric News Agency)

Xi'an Farmers Bank Opens

(Xi'an) The Xi'an branch of the Farmers Bank of the four provinces of Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Anhui opened on the morning of the 1st, issuing banknotes and hosting a banquet for people from all walks of life. (1st, Central News Agency)

(Jinan) There was heavy rain in Jinan today, with water accumulating on the roads to a depth of one foot. (1st, Special Dispatch)

(Gold and Silver)

London Gold Price Today's London gold price is 137 shillings and 1.5 pence, up 2 pence from yesterday.

London Silver Bar Today's silver price fell by .0625, spot is 19.5 pence, futures is 19.5625. The market was very quiet in the morning, and buyers were reluctant to act.

Bombay Silver Bar The Bombay silver market closed stable today, with spot falling 1 anna to 54 rupees and 5 annas, and futures also falling 1 anna.

US-UK The opening exchange rate between London and the US was 5.06375, the same as yesterday's closing price for the US-UK exchange rate. At 11:00 AM, it rose by .075 to 5.07125, with no change afterwards. At 2:00 PM, it fell by .03125 to 5.0709375. One US dollar is equivalent to 3 shillings and 11.366 pence.

UK-France This morning, foreign exchange managers sold some francs in the exchange market. The opening exchange rate between the UK and France was 76.93 francs, down 3 pounds. However, at 11:00 AM, it rose by 16 pounds to 77.09 francs, and there was no change until the time of the telegram.

Although Liverpool sold near-term cotton, the New York cotton market was stable. Brokers advised people to buy when prices fall.

UK Cotton The price for July cotton in the Liverpool cotton market at 1:00 PM was 6.02, the same as yesterday's price.

Huang Zhengqing, Security Commander of Labrang in Gansu, Will Return to Gansu Soon

(Nanjing) Huang Zhengqing, the Security Commander of Labrang in Gansu, came here two months ago to report the situation in Gansu to the Central Government and to request the Central Government to grant the title to Jamyang Hutuktu. Nanjing Municipal Public Works Bureau Opens Qinhuai River Sluice Gates

(Nanjing) The water in the Qinhuai River in Nanjing has been filled with foul odor since the beginning of summer. The Municipal Public Works Bureau opened the Dongshui Pass sluice gate on the 1st and sent Chen Qishi of the Construction Section and workers to open it. They went to the Dongguan Tou to open the sluice gate, but failed to open it because it had not been opened for many years (closed for 20 years, never opened). Then, they used an iron cable to turn the gate outside the Tongji Gate, and finally opened both the inner and outer gates together. (One-Day Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Seven-Province Locust Control Conference is scheduled to be held on the 5th at the Agricultural Experiment Institute for three days. Each province has submitted proposals. (One-Day Special Dispatch)

The Japanese Side Obstructs the Opening of the Hebei Province Special Police into the War Zone, Deliberately Making Things Difficult Regarding the Number of People and Types of Weapons. The Military Sub-Committee Sends a Telegram Calling for Lei Shourong to Return to Tianjin for Negotiations

Tianjin Correspondence: The issue of the newly formed special police team of Hebei Province entering the war zone has been negotiated with Chai Shan, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy in Beiping, for many days without any results. Yin Rugeng came to Tianjin yesterday to report this matter to Yu Xuezhong. In fact, the newly formed special police team and the security team are of a rotation nature, and there is no such thing as increasing the defense force. However, since the two matters of opening traffic and postal services in North China have not yet been realized, the Japanese side deliberately makes things difficult, and matters that are not problems become problems. In addition, the two items that the Japanese side considers to be too many people and the prohibition of machine guns from being carried into the war zone as heavy weapons are nothing more than excuses. Because the security teams of Zhou Yuying, Wei Yonghe, and Yang Yongshan, which are currently stationed in the war zone, also have more than 8,000 people and each carry machine guns. Even if the special police team does not go, the strength of the security team stationed in the war zone is also equal. It is not that after the special police team goes, our strength will increase by a certain amount. The Japanese side’s concerns are really superfluous. The provincial government currently does not take an active approach to this negotiation and intends to wait for the Military Sub-Committee to take charge. The intention of the Military Sub-Committee is that in the Tanggu Agreement, the number of special police teams in the war zone and the types of weapons that should be carried were not signed in the text of the agreement, but only orally agreed by the person in charge. As time has passed, the Japanese side deliberately refuses to recognize it because we have forgotten it. Therefore, the original person in charge must come north to contact the Japanese side in person. The original people in charge are Xiong Bin, Li Zeyi, and Lei Shourong. Xiong and Li are in Jiangxi and Fujian, respectively, and cannot go north in a short time. However, Lei Shourong has just returned to Nanjing from Japan, so a special telegram was sent to urge him to come north, intending to have Lei Shourong, based on the negotiation records of that day, resolve the matter with the Japanese side before Huang Fu returns to North China. If Lei cannot resolve it, he will wait for Huang Fu to return to assist in the handling. However, recently, Chai Shan, the military attaché of the Japanese Embassy, ​​told Yin Rugeng that this matter is of great importance and should be directly discussed with the Kwantung Army Department. Therefore, in addition to the above two methods, the Military Sub-Committee may send Lei Shourong and Yin Rugeng to Changchun to negotiate with the Kwantung Army Department of Japan as soon as possible. As for the newly formed special police team, they are still stationed in Cainancun and Cangxian in southern Tianjin, training every day, waiting for the order to be mobilized. However, according to observation, before the opening of traffic and postal services is realized, they will still not be able to enter the war zone for a while. The Japanese side has other deep intentions, which is to benefit the chaos in our war zone and disadvantage our order.

Although the strength of the new special police may not be greater than that of the security team currently stationed in the war zone, they are all stronger than half-year police training. Their knowledge of security law and police law is of course better than that of the security team. Recently, the war zone has become a hotbed of crime. The special police team will naturally have to crack down on it, and the backgrounds of all the hotbeds are Japanese and Korean vagrants, which will inevitably cause some inconvenience. Wu Minghao, the Magistrate of Jixian County, came to Tianjin yesterday to report to the provincial government on the withdrawal of the Japanese army from the county. He said that although the Japanese army has withdrawn, it has set up a military long-distance telephone between Malanyu and Jixian, and the news is still more sensitive than ours. There are countless drug agencies and gambling houses in the local area, all opened by Japanese and Korean people. Farmers are tempted and fall into depravity more and more every day. The fields are barren and left unattended, resulting in the complete bankruptcy of the rural economy. So far, the summer field tax has not yet been levied, and the county government has no way to rectify and relieve the situation. It is hoped that the special police team will go in as soon as possible to assist the local administrative agencies in persuasion so that the villages will not be completely destroyed. As evidenced by this statement, it is even more evident that the Japanese side’s obstruction of our special police’s entry into the war zone has other unspeakable motives. (May 29)

France in the Tense European Situation (French Correspondence) Parliamentary Politics is Gradually Disintegrating, Doumergue's Cabinet Inclines to Dictatorship

The European political situation is turbulent and unstable. The Disarmament Conference has no results. The main reason is that the confrontation between France and Germany has become increasingly intensified. At the same time, Italy wants to divide the hegemony of Central Europe. Therefore, French diplomacy has become even more tense. Not only must Germany not be allowed to use international diplomacy to restore its past strength, but also to share its strength to deal with Italy. However, within France, in terms of economy, it could only barely maintain from declining in the past. This year's economic situation has deteriorated very seriously. Leaving aside the general economic situation, just looking at the state treasury revenue, the amount of revenue shortfall this year is 700,000 francs. This shows the seriousness of France's financial problems, which is also a major problem in France's internal affairs.

The Paris riots on February 6th were the most significant event since the fall of Napoleon III and the establishment of the Third Republic in 1870. However, this riot was limited to the city of Paris. Similar movements did not occur simultaneously in other places, so the government still had means of suppression. The foundation of the Republic was not shaken by the disturbance of the royalists. As for the Stavisky-type fraud cases, they have occurred many times in France in the past century, so they are not considered a major problem. Of course, the royalists and communists can use this to stir up a movement, and many people in the public sympathize with them. However, to eliminate the evil forces of society, there is no need

to fundamentally overthrow the current system. We examine the violence used by the demonstrators. Their weapons are nothing more than knives and small

stones, which can also measure the public's feelings. Therefore, former President Doumergue, at the age of 72, took on the arduous task. As an old politician, he served as the prime minister in a time of crisis. First, he asked the leaders of all parties to "end all political disputes from now on." He also put forward hope conditions in the parliament, asking the House of Representatives to "indicate that such a foolish situation will not continue to occur for the sake of France's political stability." As a result, he gained the trust of the parliament. From mid-March to mid-May, the House of Representatives adjourned for two months, which means that the government was not interfered with by the parliament and actually achieved budget savings. Like changes in tariff rates, the dictatorial power of France has been gradually disintegrating in the past three years. There are too many parties, which cannot exert the role of the parliament and cannot make politics relatively stable. Whether Doumergue's cabinet's dictatorship will cause France's political situation to turn into fascist politics due to the stimulation of diplomatic tension is still a question.

The general public in France has very well-developed ideas of freedom and equality.

In the past, they have paid huge sacrifices for political freedom. As the leader of the left-wing party Herriot said, "We want to challenge the dictatorial political ideology that is sweeping the world without pretense, because dictatorial politics is enough to threaten political freedom internally and hinder international peace externally..." The parliamentary politics of France has indeed exposed its shortcomings. However, in politics, the President of France is only a head of state equal to a puppet. Although he has the power to dissolve the parliament in the constitution, since President MacMahon tried it once in 1877 and failed, there has been no second dissolution of the parliament. Therefore, no matter how the cabinet is formed, if it encounters a vote of no confidence in the parliament, it cannot dissolve the parliament and re-elect to ask the people's true intentions. There is only one way to resign from the cabinet. With this foundation, even if French politics has a dictatorial tendency, its nature is of a different type. What's more, Doumergue himself is different from Hitler and Mussolini, so Doumergue's dictatorship will not develop as unrestricted as in Italy and Germany.

In short, the current emergency cabinet in France has a strong dictatorial flavor. Its main purpose is to calm domestic unrest and maintain the status quo. As for the international aspect, she will do her best to maintain her existing position, even at a considerable cost, sacrificing past prejudices, in order to consolidate her international position, such as being friendly with the Soviet Union to suppress Germany and to restrict Italy. The general situation in the international community is largely returning to the diplomatic situation before 1914. The domestic trend is that the image of parliamentary politics is gradually fading in France. (April 26, Paris)

Bizarre Phenomenon of Black Soil Under Japanese Rule

(Opium and Gambling are Public, Brothels are Everywhere)

(Japanese Vagrants Roam Everywhere)

According to people from Heilongjiang Province, since the Dragon River Province was ruled by the Japanese, opium and gambling have been made public and brothels have sprung up everywhere. Generally, pseudo-government officials and dandies either go to opium dens to smoke and exhale, or go to brothels to indulge in wine and women to have fun. The Dragon River in broad daylight has been transformed into a world of opium and sex. If this continues, the compatriots in the Northeast will become more and more degenerate, and their spirits and bodies will become more and more fragile. I am afraid that there will never be any hope of restoring the homeland. This kind of deadly poison is worse than airplanes and cannons.

Officials of various agencies can record their accounts when they usually go to opium dens to smoke opium or stay in brothels with prostitutes. They do not need to pay in cash. At the end of each month, the persons in charge of the opium dens and brothels will settle the accounts, send them to the various agencies separately, and deduct the amount of opium money and brothel money owed by each official from the salaries of the various agencies. This kind of opium fee and prostitution fee is the largest monthly expense for officials of various agencies, and there are often those who do not have enough household expenses. As for those who open opium dens, most of them are Koreans, and those who open brothels are mostly Japanese. Observing their intentions, they want to use chronic poison to absorb the marrow of our nation, so that our people will become weak until they are destroyed. What is even more bizarre is that Japanese vagrants roam everywhere. They often ride horses directly into the classrooms of the Women's Normal School after being drunk, revealing all kinds of ugly states and uttering all kinds of irregular languages. Because of this, many female students have not dared to go to school for many days. All kinds of bizarre phenomena are everywhere. There are too many to write down. The taste of being a slave in a lost province makes people feel very sad. (Northeast News Agency)

Mao Zedong Has Been Bombed to Death, The Internal Disintegration of the Red Bandits Has No Fighting Spirit, The Ring Leader Has Been Executed, The Remaining Bandits Are Even More Insufficient to Be Eliminated

Nanchang Communication, Military News, when the 8th Column of the National Army was ordered to recover Jianning the previous time, the pseudo 135th Army Corps was entrenched in the north of Jianning City. The National Army first attacked and advanced against the 2nd Division of the pseudo-army stationed in Mazhai. They charged each other more than ten times. The bandits could not support it and all collapsed in the southwest direction of Jianning. The bandits abandoned and did not defend the Jianning city walls. According to the captured bandit soldiers, since the fifth encirclement and suppression by the National Army, the officers and soldiers of the bandit army have suffered heavy casualties, especially the lack of ammunition. Each gun has at most four or five rows, so they dare not linger at all in every battle. Once they have the opportunity, they will retreat. A few days ago, Mao Zedong was bombed to death by the National Army's plane in the rear of Ruijin. The bandit troops' replenishment of conscription, ammunition, food, and all daily necessities are extremely difficult. After Mao Zedong's death, the internal spirit was disintegrating and the bandit officers and soldiers had no fighting spirit. Therefore, in recent battles, officers and soldiers were unwilling to flee with them, hid in the mountains, and surrendered as soon as the National Army chased after them. Commander Zhou has reported to the higher-level agencies after taking the statement.

In addition, the division commander Li Mo'an telegraphed on the 26th saying that the division has been winning battles in bandit suppression recently. Recently, it has approached the vicinity of Shuinan, and the bunker line between Guangchang and Jianning has been effectively broken and the remaining bandits have been driven to the south of the line. The internal collapse of the bandits and the escape is extremely chaotic. According to the captured bandits, Mao Zedong has indeed been bombed to death. The red flag, red star, and red army newspapers have had no mention of Mao for days, I think the ring leader has been executed, and the remaining bandits are even more insufficient to be eliminated. (May 30, Datong News Agency)

Fang Bandit Plans to Flee to Northern Jiangxi, Chen and Zhao's Troops Advance and Suppress

Nanchang dispatch: Fang Zhimin's bandits have recently expanded the pseudo-independent regiments and guerrilla forces in the counties along the Xin River and Rao River basins. The pseudo-independent 1st, 2nd, and 3rd columns, reorganized from the independent regiments of Guixi and Shangrao, fled to western Zhejiang and southern Anhui. Currently, in Wannian and Fuliang, scattered bandits are causing disturbances everywhere, rumors are rampant, and people are panicking. Recovery of Feiyuan in Eastern Jiangxi; Bandit Attack on Tongbu Repelled

Wuyuan dispatch: Regarding the military operations to suppress the Red bandits in eastern Jiangxi, in addition to the eastern route Zhao Guantao's troops, Liang's division, and Zhao's brigade recovering Hengfeng on May 25, military operations on the Jiangxi-Anhui border have also made continuous progress. After sending troops to attack from the flanks, the bandits began to collapse and retreat to the high mountains north of Biaoxi. That evening, Feiyuan was recovered. Currently, they are reorganizing and building blockhouses. According to captured bandits, the bandits suffered about 400 casualties in this battle. The national army also suffered some casualties due to the uphill attack. Furthermore, at 4:00 AM on the 23rd, about 400 bandits, with about 300 guns, launched a fierce attack on the national army's blockhouses in Tongbu, Nanhe, Dexing. The two sides engaged in a fierce battle for 30 minutes, killing two bandits, wounding dozens, and capturing one wounded bandit, one rifle, and dozens of bullets. The bandits retreated to Dada, about 500 meters southwest of Tongbu, intending to stubbornly resist.
