Feng Yuxiang Returns to Tai'an, Visits Fan Zhongyan Ancestral Hall in Qingzhou, and Encourages Elementary School Students to Resist Japan

Jinan dispatch: Feng Yuxiang has toured the famous scenic spots in eastern Shandong for over ten days. Then, as his enthusiasm for travel waned, he returned to Tai'an. On May 29, he arrived in Weixian from Yantai. On the morning of the 30th, he left Weixian by car. When passing through Qingzhou, he got off the car to pay respects to the portrait of Fan Zhongyan and gave a speech at the Tenth Middle School. At 6:10 PM, he arrived in Jinan. Important figures welcomed him at the station. After a short stay, the car switched from the Jiaoji Railway to the Jinpu Railway and immediately returned to Tai'an. The details of his return from Weifang to Jinan are as follows:

The special car sent by Han Fuqu to welcome Feng arrived in Weixian on the 29th. At 5:00 AM on the 30th, Feng's guards moved the luggage onto the car. County Magistrate Li Wenli, Police Chief Zhang En'yuan, Brigade Commander Li Xiangchen, and Regiment Commander Chuan Jianheng all waited at Feng's residence in the Shanghai Company to see him off. Zhang Yunmen, an old Christian friend from Guangwen Middle School in Dongguan, and Principal Cui Hongze also came to the station to see him off. Feng bought sesame cakes, fried dough sticks, and eggs, and let the people who were seeing him off feast on them. At 6:45 AM, Feng boarded the car. Amidst the cheers of the crowd, the car slowly departed. Weixian is very close to Qingzhou. At 8:00 AM, he arrived in Qingzhou. County Magistrate Yang Jiuwu, Police Chief Ma Dianbang, and Regiment Commander Hou Zhaolin led a company of pistol guards to provide security at the station. After the car stopped, Yang Jiuwu and Hou Zhaolin boarded the car to welcome him. Feng asked if there were any places to visit in Qingzhou. Yang replied that there was Fan Wenzheng's pavilion and his portrait west of the city, and Yunmen Mountain south of the city, which are also famous scenic spots in the county, and both are worth visiting. Because Feng admired Fan Wenzheng, he got out of the car to visit. He borrowed a long-distance bus from the automobile bureau. The station to Fan Gong Pavilion is about six or seven li. Feng arrived and paid respects to Fan Gong's statue. The core area is close to the Nanyang River, the water flows gurgling, and the scenery is beautiful. Feng drank tea and rested here for a while, then took a car into the city to rest at the Tenth Middle School. Principal Zhu Junsheng invited Feng to speak to the students. Feng declined but could not refuse, so he agreed. He then gathered more than a thousand students from the Tenth Middle School, the Tenth Middle School branch, the Fourth Normal School, and the Fourth Normal School Affiliated Elementary School to listen to the lecture at the Tenth Middle School. Before the students gathered, Feng wrote the words "Give Me Back My Rivers and Mountains" on a horizontal plaque and a couplet: "Rescuing the people has no day of rest; Revolution is the ultimate person." He instructed the school to hang them up as a motto. After a while, the students gathered in the main hall. Feng took the stage to speak, describing the seriousness of the national crisis and the situation of resisting Japan, in a tragic and impassioned manner.

Mr. Feng returned to the station. At the invitation of Lu Wenyuan, the section chief of the Jiaoji Railway Works Section, he went to the Works Section office to rest. Lu Wenyuan runs a private elementary school next to the station, which is dedicated to admitting the children of railway employees. There are hundreds of students, and the results are very good. He specially invited Mr. Feng to give a speech to the elementary school. Feng agreed readily. After resting for a while, he went to the school. The students were all around ten years old and welcomed him outside the school in a lively and orderly manner. Feng was very happy to see this. Then the students filed into the classroom, and nearby people also poured in to listen to the lecture, with no space inside or outside the room. After a brief introduction by the principal, Feng spoke, briefly saying: "Section Chief, teachers, little brothers and sisters, today I have the opportunity to speak to you in such a nice house. I think it is a very good scene and a very rare opportunity. I feel very happy and joyful. The principal just gave a brief introduction. I'm afraid you little brothers and sisters still don't know who I am. I am Feng Yuxiang. I studied in Mount Tai and came down the mountain to see all parts of Jiaodong. Wherever I go, I talk about resisting Japanese imperialism because Japan bullies our nation and invades our country. I am thoroughly opposed to the idea of non-resistance. Anyone who does not resist is our enemy. Do you all understand?" (The students answered loudly, "Yes!") "Just now I heard your principal say that you are all children of railway employees. I thought of a story to tell you. There was a person whose son graduated from higher elementary school. He wanted to ask him to work, so he took him to see a teacher to ask for advice. The teacher told him that if you want to succeed in your career, you only need two things: first, you must have the identity of a poor child; second, you must be determined to be the first person. The name of this teacher, I will tell you later. When he was young, his family was very poor. From the age of six or seven, he often heard his parents say, 'What are we going to eat tomorrow? What are we going to take to the pawnshop tomorrow?' He was immersed in this kind of life all day long. Over time, it made him determined to work hard in the future to avoid the pressure of life. When he was eleven years old, he began to work for others. The job was to mop the floor. When he was mopping the floor, he was determined to be the first person to mop the floor, mopping it white, bright, clean, and fast. No one nearby could compare to him. At the age of fourteen, he was promoted to deliver letters, and on the first day of delivering letters, he was determined to be the first person in delivering letters, the fastest and most reliable, never sending the wrong letter. Four months later, he memorized all the streets, alleys, doors, and even the number of people living in each door, and everyone's name clearly. When he received the letter, he could deliver it very quickly and accurately. As expected, he became the first person in delivering letters, and everyone praised him. At the age of seventeen, he was promoted to the telegraph bureau to learn to send telegrams. He worked hard day and night and became the first person among the telegraph students. Later, in every job he did, he was determined to be the first person until he made the steel industry and became the steel king. Who is this person? It is the American steel king Carnegie. Now that he is doing charity, he is determined to be the first person in the world in charity, using all his money to build nursing homes, orphanages, hospitals, and other causes. So someone asked him, and he said that to be successful in business, the first thing is to have the qualifications of a poor child, and the second is to be determined to be the first person. He said that rich people have reliance and bad habits and cannot do things, while poor children are like a clean white paper. I said just now that we are resisting Japan, because if we don't resist Japan, we will perish as a nation. I hope you will be determined to become the first person to resist Japanese imperialism, the first person to recover the lost land by force. Do you understand?" The students answered yes and repeated the main points of the speech to the students (the answers were very orderly.) "Since everyone understands, goodbye!"

At 1:48 PM, the train left Qingzhou. It stopped briefly at Zhangdian to load coal and water and then continued on its way. When it arrived in Zhoucun, Cao Fulin, the commander of the 29th Division, had already arrived in Jinan. The Chief of Staff Wang Shiqi led officers to welcome him at the station. After the car stopped, Wang boarded the car and talked with Feng for a few words. The car continued to travel west. At 6:10 PM, the car arrived in Jinan. Han Fuqu, Zhang Liansheng, Guo Zhigang, Sha Yuebo, Wen Chenglie, Liu Xizhong, Wang Kairu, and others all came to the station to welcome him. After the car stopped, Han and others boarded the car for a short conversation. Han asked why he didn't stay a few more days in Yantai, where the scenery is very beautiful. Feng said that there were many rumors in Yantai, and the news was not very accurate, so it was better to return to Mount Tai. Han asked him to stay in Jinan for a few days, but Feng refused, so as not to delay everyone's work. He also said that the eastern Shandong area is rich and prosperous, and its villages are even better than the county towns in western Shandong. He visited the Qi Gong Ancestral Hall in Penglai and the Beiwo City. He paid respects to the three memorial tablets of Ding Ruchang and others who died for the country in the Sino-Japanese War in Weihai. They are all anti-Japanese martyrs and are worthy of respect. Today, he passed through Qingzhou and visited the Fan Gong Ancestral Hall. Fan Gong's "worrying before the world and enjoying after the world" is even more admirable. He also visited the Three Sages Ancestral Hall. Furthermore, there are many products along the coast. Changshan Islands produces a lot of sea cucumbers. The Japanese use a big head, shaped like a tube, and enter the sea, and people can enter it to change the air and get the most sea cucumbers. Our fishermen still swim to collect sea cucumbers, so they get the least. Now, local fishermen have also purchased a dozen big heads and are imitating them. Each one costs 400 yuan. Then Han and others got out of the car. At 6:40 PM, Feng continued to leave Jinan by car. He can arrive in Tai'an around 9:00 PM and live in the original place. (May 31)

Anhui Province Bans Gangs; Civil Affairs Department Orders County Magistrates to Handle Seriously

Anqing dispatch: The Anhui Civil Affairs Department recently received a report from Qu Zhuxun, the county magistrate of Suxian, stating that he was ordered to investigate and ban the Guangdan Society and implement the joint responsibility system for Baojia chiefs. After investigation, although the names of the Anqing Gang, Qinghong Gang, Wuji Tao, and other gangs are different from the Guangdan Society, their ability to hinder local order and tranquility all make them possible dens for bandits. In order to strictly control mass organizations and prevent problems before they arise, it is planned to ban them uniformly by analogy. In addition to ordering each district and posting announcements to all Baojia chiefs to inform them, we have submitted a written report on the implementation of the order to ban the Guangdan Society and, by analogy, to ban the Anqing Gang, Qinghong Gang, Wuji Tao, and other circumstances. Please review and approve for implementation. The Civil Affairs Department immediately issued instructions: "Noted. There are many local gangs. The county magistrate, considering that the names of the Anqing Gang, Qinghong Gang, Wuji Tao, etc., all have the possibility of being dens for bandits, plans to ban them uniformly by analogy, which is correct. In addition to ordering each county to do the same, you must still earnestly investigate and ban them to curb the emergence of chaos." Furthermore, it ordered all counties that such wicked people are everywhere. If they are not prevented in advance and strictly prohibited, they will cause harm to the local area in the future, which is no small matter. It is urgently ordered that the county magistrate instruct the district Baojia chiefs and security teams under their jurisdiction to earnestly investigate and ban these illegal organizations without any concealment and report the implementation situation to the authorities for review at any time. (May 30)

Songjiang

Method for Centralizing County Expenses in the County Treasury

The county government previously received instructions from the Finance Department, promulgating the "Methods for the Establishment of County Treasury, County Funds Revenue and Expenditure Storage, and Various Forms," requiring implementation from the 23rd year onwards. After receiving the document, County Magistrate Jin believed that the situation in this county was complicated and the procedures for handling this matter were cumbersome. Therefore, he convened a meeting of relevant agencies and groups the other day, with County Magistrate Jin presiding, reading out the department's order and the promulgated regulations. After detailed discussion by the public, the following methods were resolved: (A) Practical methods: (1) All county funds in this county shall be deposited into the county treasury in accordance with the department's order from July 1, the 13th year onwards. (2) All agencies in this county shall settle all kinds of funds for various years ending in the 22nd year (June 30, the 23rd year) and deposit them into the county treasury before July 15. (3) Various types of county funds collected or received by various agencies: 1. In the county government: county regular tax, various mu surtaxes, deed tax surtaxes, dental tax construction fees, slaughter tax education fees, construction fees, vehicle tax, building permit fees, Tinglin Shantang subsidy education fees, various miscellaneous surtaxes. 2. In the Education Bureau: tuition fees, land rent, original fund interest. 3. Fines for violations of police regulations in the Public Security Bureau. 4. Various rental income from the Asset Management Office. 5. Production income from the Agricultural Extension Office. 6. Various rental income from the district offices. (4) Various types of donations and taxes that various agencies should transfer to the county government for collection from the 23rd year onwards: 1. County regular tax, mu surtax, slaughter tax education fees, stove tax salt jin price increase, bamboo specialty tax, cotton rapeseed tax, and Tinglin Shantang subsidy education fees of the Education Bureau. 2. County regular tax and mu surtax of the Asset Management Office. 3. Various miscellaneous surtaxes from the district offices. (5) From the 23rd year onwards, all procedures for paying and receiving funds shall be handled in accordance with the department's order. (B) Matters to be submitted for explanation: (1) Before the county budget for the 23rd year is approved, will the expenses of various agencies be paid according to the budget amount? (2) When there are insufficient funds in the treasury, can overdrafts be made from the county treasury? There are also four points of suggestions on unifying revenue and expenditure, which will be submitted by the county to the department for approval. According to instructions, the County Treasury is undertaken by the Songjiang Farmers Branch.

Water Police Team Captures Thieves

Fan Zhicheng, the captain of the first team of the Provincial Water Police Team, received a report that Wang Jinqing's family robbery case in Fengjing Dongzhaikou, Songyi, was related to Li A'er. He immediately sent detectives to Daoyuan Town, Fengxian County, to arrest Li and escort him back to the Zhujing team headquarters for interrogation. At first, Li's confession was cunning, denying the surname Li, saying that his real name was Shen Lanchun, 38 years old, and he did not dare to break the law. After further questioning, he finally confessed truthfully and bowed his head without words. In addition to robbing Wang Jinqing's family in Dongzhai, Li A'er also robbed rice boats in Wuku Xinzhen and other cases repeatedly. The confession was recorded and handed over to Songjiang today, and sub-team leader Hu Tu was ordered to hand it over to the county government for handling.

Fengxian

Vigorous Land Survey

This county began preparing for land survey in July of the 21st year. The Land Bureau was established in October of the 22nd year, and it has been actively working to urge landowners to clear and survey the land, proceeding in stages. In only seven or eight months, more than forty townships have completed the survey, and more than ten townships are still surveying and have not yet been completed. To summarize the land survey of the entire county, one-third has already been completed. It is heard that the province will issue a new land survey method to thoroughly change it. The county party department specially presented a request to the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department yesterday, to forward it to the provincial government, ordering the Provincial Land Bureau not to change the method to facilitate the land survey so that it can be completed as soon as possible.

Suzhou

Garment Makers Oppose Forming a Trade Association and Go on Strike

There are more than 40,000 tailors in Suzhou City, divided into four gangs: Changshu, Danyang, Zhenjiang, and Taixing. Among them, the Changshu and Danyang gangs account for the most. There are also many people from Wuxi and local areas. There is a Xuanyuan Guild Hall in Jiusheng Lane, which is the industry's public property. There are no other trade association organizations. Recently, someone named Chen and others applied to the county government for approval to establish a garment industry trade association. In addition to collecting nine jiao of foreign money per table per month, they also cracked down on light materials (it is customary for tailors to steal materials when making clothes, otherwise, the patrons must pay for wine. Light materials are to eliminate this bad habit), reduce wages, and make work at 60% of the market price (for example, a single-layer cheongsam originally cost two yuan and eight jiao, but it was reduced to one yuan and fifty-six jiao). The industry believes that this has a direct impact on their interests and hinders the lives of workers, and they expressed their opposition. They suddenly went on strike yesterday (the 1st) morning, and gathered more than 2,000 people to hold a meeting in the guild hall in Guanjian Jiusheng Lane. At the same time, a part of the workers, holding small flags, went to the shops that had not gone on strike to persuade them to join the strike, and nominated Qu Wenxiu, Gao Yongqing, Dai Ziqing, Li Nianxiu, Jin Afu, Chen Guisheng, and other thirty or forty people as representatives to petition the county party department. The county party department convened a meeting of all relevant parties to mediate, and persuaded them to resume work. If they need to join the trade association, they can first have the industry rush to create a list of members to join, and then have the members hold a general meeting to formulate industry rules. Then, the lawyer Xie Jusan, hired by the industry, stated that he was dissatisfied with the trade association and hoped that a majority of genuine industry members would form another trade association. As of 3:00 PM, there were still no results.

Long-distance telephone message: At 4:00 PM, about 3,000 to 4,000 workers (including shop owners and workers) gathered at the trade association on Jingde Road. Traffic from the west entrance of Guanjian Street to the Jingde Road area was completely blocked. At that time, the workers had a major conflict with the trade association. Several officers and soldiers suppressing the scene were injured, and the gate of the trade association was also knocked down. After hearing the news, Police Chief Shen Gaoqin immediately led the police to persuade them. They dispersed at 6:00 PM. After the incident, Chief Shen heard people say that ax gangs participated in the incident, and three workers were injured by axes. Therefore, he went to the trade association again to search and took Chen Yulin (not a garment shop owner), the initiator of the trade association, to the bureau for questioning. At 7:00 PM in the evening, another group of workers went to the trade association to negotiate, but did not cause any trouble. As of the time of the message, there were still more than a hundred people gathered in front of the trade association.

The Verdict on the Appeal of the Defendants in the Xin Renhe Case

The case of Sun Xingsheng, the owner of the Shanghai Xin Renhe ship, plotting to kill the peddler Ma Kou and five others, was appealed to the Suzhou High Court. Yesterday (the 1st), the Third Criminal Court conducted the trial. The original judgment on the crimes of Sun Xingsheng and others was revoked. Sun Xingsheng was sentenced to imprisonment for jointly plotting murder. Shen Xingqiao, Shen Chuanlang, Wang Mingda, and Huang Fusheng were each sentenced to 20 years imprisonment for conspiring to murder. Guo Xihou and Lu Ronggeng were each sentenced to 10 years imprisonment for conspiring to murder. Zhang Xiao Zhang and Feng Fusheng were each sentenced to 2 years imprisonment for conspiring to murder. Zhang Xiao Zhang was given a three-year reprieve. Feng Fusheng's public prosecution was not accepted. The attached civil lawsuit appeal ruling was sent to the Civil Court of this court for trial.

Jiading

County Government Strictly Prohibits Dragon Boats

County Magistrate Xu Cixuan heard that some well-meaning people were preparing to race dragon boats on the abolished lunar Duanwu Festival. He issued a notice in advance strictly prohibiting it. If anyone dared to violate it, they would be severely punished. On the 28th, the Party-Government Talk Conference raised it again. After discussion by various agencies, it was resolved to thoroughly investigate and ban it. The day before yesterday, he also issued a notice to all township chiefs to strictly investigate and report, and the Public Security Bureau ordered the police in the urban and rural areas and the owners of various shipyards to make it clear and instruct them, and to submit a guarantee that they will never participate in or repair or build dragon boats in their respective jurisdictions, so that they cannot proceed.

Provincial Approval for Maintaining Land Survey

More than 20 agencies and groups, including the County Asset Management Office, previously jointly telegraphed the provincial government to request that the original plan be continued because the Provincial Land Bureau changed the land survey plan and disregarded the purpose of the landowners clearing the boundaries. The provincial government approved the following: "The telegram has been noted. This province previously received a telegram from Chiang Kai-shek, the chairman of the Military Affairs Committee, ordering that the initial work of the land survey must be completed before the end of March in the 24th year, so the original plan was slightly improved in order to quickly go to the matter and accomplish the great cause early. The land survey is one of the predetermined tasks. Although the implementation steps have been slightly improved, the purpose of urgently resolving land disputes and completing the consolidation work as soon as possible is the same as what the people of the county expect. As for the layer of people's own written reports, its original intention is to make people participate in the work so that the boundaries of the land are more accurate and the speed of business is further increased. The technical methods are still the responsibility of the land survey team, which is no different from the original method. As for the funding layer, it is still allocated according to the original plan, and there is no extra burden on the people. You must understand this purpose well and jointly promote this matter."

District Division Dispute Resolved

The county government was ordered to merge autonomous regions and organized a district division committee. The first resolution was to maintain the original eight districts and submitted it to the Civil Affairs Department for approval. The Civil Affairs Department ordered that there should be at least six districts. After discussion, it was resolved that the original seventh district would be merged into the second district, and the original six or seven districts and the Fangtai and other three townships in the first district would be merged into the sixth district. However, the Huangdu, Anting, and Fangtai towns in the district each strongly advocated setting up a district office in their respective towns, and the competition was fierce and could not be resolved. It was resolved that each town should submit a written reason for further review. On the 29th, a continued meeting was held. The parties still insisted on their own opinions. Finally, it was decided that the original sixth district would be merged into the 区 district, the original eighth district would be merged into the fourth district, and the Fangtai and other three townships would still be under the first district. The plan was to merge the entire county into five districts. The parties had no objection, and the dispute was resolved.

Haimen

Lingdian Port Sampan Men Cause Trouble

The other day (27th), the Baofeng ship came from Shanghai to Haimen. When it arrived at Lingdian Port in the sixth district, many sampans leaned against the ship to compete for passengers. Among them, sampan man Wen Guangxian had a conflict with Chen A'er, a small worker on the ship, over a trivial matter. Chen was stabbed in the left neck by Wen with a bamboo pole, and blood flowed like a fountain. He fell to the ground in extreme pain. Then all the small workers were furious and planned to throw Wen into the river. At that time, Yuan Liuqing, the district chief of the sixth district, was on the ship and strongly dissuaded them, promising to investigate and deal with Wen according to the law after arriving ashore. The small workers obeyed and retreated. Later, Chen A'er was taken to Shanghai by the ship for treatment, but the injury was quite serious, and there was a risk to his life.

Wuxi

Variable Readjustment of Cocoon Transaction Control

In order to thoroughly reform sericulture, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction specially promulgated measures for the control of cocoon transactions. It was decided that these measures would be implemented during the current spring cocoon season. However, various cocoon merchants have found many conflicts between these measures and the original regulations for cocoon transactions, raising objections. After repeated meetings and separate submissions to the Yuan, the Ministry, and the Provincial Department, they requested that the measures be changed; otherwise, they vowed not to pay the three-yuan improvement fee. Simultaneously, the trade association continued to petition the sericulture model district. The director and deputy director of the model district, Yan Shenyu and Cai Jingde, also felt that the spring cocoon season was approaching rapidly and an appropriate solution should be sought promptly to avoid problems arising at the last minute. Yesterday, they drafted opinions and jointly went to the provincial capital to request instructions. These are excerpted as follows:

(1) The cocoon industry association's previous request to postpone the implementation of cocoon transaction control has not yet been approved by the Ministry and the Province. However, the spring cocoon season is imminent. If the government and merchants remain deadlocked, problems will inevitably arise. Therefore, three opinions are proposed: A. For cocoon processing units with four or fewer stoves and those that have not opened for weighing for two consecutive years, special consideration should be given to allow them to operate. B. For all cocoon processing units that open for weighing, they should still follow the established practice of registering with the association. The business owners who open for business should voluntarily waive the provision in Article 4 of the control measures regarding the distribution of profits to stove workers. However, the registration deposit should be specially exempted. C. Before cocoon merchants ship dried cocoons, the association will be responsible for encouraging them to pay an improvement fee of three yuan per dried cocoon load. Director Yan and Deputy Director Cai believe that the above measures seem feasible and have gone to the province to request instructions before making a final decision.

(2) It has been decided that silkworm seed control will be implemented in the autumn season of this year. Yesterday, the model district issued a public notice stating that all improved silkworm seeds will be managed by the model district, directly distributed to silkworm farmers, and merchants are not allowed to buy or sell them. It is also stipulated that the price of each autumn seed sheet is five jiao. However, the selling price at the seed farm must be at least eight jiao and five fen per sheet. The deficit of three jiao and five fen will be subsidized from the collected improvement fees. Tang Xixiang, the director of the sericulture testing field stationed in the province, has received instructions from Director Shen of the Department of Construction that the province has decided to allocate 300,000 yuan in advance to purchase autumn seeds from seed farms, which will be reimbursed from the improvement fees in the future.

(3) Now that seed prices have been lowered, the number of silkworm farmers will inevitably increase. Whether there will be enough mulberry leaves will become a problem. Director Shen has ordered the sericulture testing field to conduct a thorough survey of mulberry leaf production. After statistics are available, silkworm seeds will be issued according to the amount.

A Good Opportunity for the Development of Chinese Silk

The New York Mercantile Exchange previously only allowed Japanese silk to be traded, which aroused strong opposition from the Chinese silk industry. However, due to the encirclement by Japanese merchants, this did not materialize, leading to the further decline of Chinese silk. Now, the exchange will vote to resolve the issue of whether Chinese and Italian silk can be traded on the exchange. If this is realized, it will provide a good opportunity for the development of Chinese silk. Zeng Yangfu, the chairman of the Sericulture Improvement Committee of the National Economic Council, has already telegraphed the NEC to forward a telegram to the Chinese ambassador to the United States and the consul in New York, requesting them to visit the exchange and influential figures in the American silk industry to explain the advantages and disadvantages in detail in order to achieve this goal. He also telegraphed the national silk industry to strive for it together. Qian Fenghao, the chairman of the Wuxi Silk Factory Trade Association, received Zeng's telegram yesterday and immediately telegraphed the NEC and the Sericulture Improvement Committee, requesting them to strive for it together.

Stone Worker Stabbed to Death in the Dark While Attempting Rape

Chen Desheng from Dongtai, 43 years old, was a helmsman on patrol boat No. 3 of the 2nd squad of the 10th team of the waterside police force stationed in Wuxi. His wife, Xuan, 44 years old, is now a female worker quarrying yellow stone at Baogei Mountain in the 3rd district of this county (preparing for the construction of the around-the-lake road). They have a son and a daughter. The son, Chunbao, 21 years old, also serves in the waterside police. The daughter, Guibao, 17 years old, lives with her mother near Qingqi Township, Baogei Mountain. The day before yesterday, Desheng took three days of leave to return home to enjoy family time with his wife and daughter. Yesterday (the 1st) morning, at about one o'clock, Desheng was sound asleep with his wife and daughter when Zhou Qunshan, a fellow villager (also a worker quarrying yellow stone there), carrying two daggers, secretly entered Chen's house and attempted to rape Xuan. When Xuan refused, Zhou immediately drew a dagger and stabbed her left knee, creating a wound about half an inch long and two or three fen deep. Xuan cried out in pain, waking Desheng. Desheng immediately got up and fought Qunshan in the dark. Both daggers in Qunshan's hands were taken away by Desheng. Desheng then stabbed Qunshan wildly, causing blood to flow. Knowing that he was no match, Qunshan fled out the door. However, because he was severely injured, he collapsed in a wheat field by the roadside after walking only a dozen steps. At that time, nearby male and female workers had come out after hearing the noise. Seeing the situation, they immediately watched over Chen Desheng and his wife, along with their daughter Guibao. After dawn, they were tied up and sent to the 2nd police substation of the 8th public security precinct. The patrol officer, Cao Shengxian, held a preliminary hearing and ordered them all to be temporarily detained, awaiting transfer to the city for legal proceedings. Meanwhile, Su Shifa, the head of the 263rd district, came to the city to report to the local branch court, requesting an examination of Zhou Qunshan's body, and notified Qunshan's brother, Cunfa, to come to the village to handle the matter.

Jiangyin

Unified Collection of Local Miscellaneous Taxes

The county government, upon the order of the Department of Finance, is reorganizing the unified collection of local miscellaneous taxes. It specially summoned various collection agencies and held a meeting at the county government the day before yesterday and made the following decisions: (1) From July 1st, the county will print receipts for all miscellaneous taxes and issue them to the original collecting agencies for collection. At the end of each month, quarter, or year, according to the collection period, the receipts will be submitted and delivered to the county government for receipt. (2) The security donation will be collected by the district regiment headquarters and submitted on schedule. (3) Each agency should send the original receipt format to the county for reference so that a new receipt format can be determined. (4) The house tax will be collected jointly by the 1st district public office and the education property management office. (5) If the miscellaneous taxes were previously submitted to the property office or collected by the county government and included in the county funds for overall distribution, they should all be submitted to the county in the future and transferred to the county treasury. If the miscellaneous taxes were collected and used by each agency themselves, the collected donations should be submitted to the county government and then reclaimed by the original agency upon presentation of a receipt. (6) The public security bureau is required to submit at least 500 yuan per month for the store tax. If the amount collected is insufficient, the bureau will be liable for the difference, which will be deducted when the funds are issued. All surplus funds will be submitted in full.

Yangzhou

Resumption of Business in Shierwei

The boatmen and workers of Shierwei, who were competing between steamers and sailing vessels, sent representatives to Beijing to petition. Because they did not get what they wanted, a general strike was triggered. The Ministry of Finance ordered the public offices on both sides of the river to reallocate 100 steamer tickets for the Xiang shore and completely convert 200 small steamer tickets for the Wan shore to sailing vessels. According to Zheng Funan of the Lianghuai Salt Affairs Office, who returned to Yangzhou from Shierwei, the merchants have all reopened for business, but the salt workers have not yet indicated that they will resume work.

Jiashan

Tragic Suicide of an Elementary School Teacher Due to Unpaid Salary

The financial difficulties of the county's education funds have reached an extreme point. Xu Zhaozong, the director of the education bureau, has recently mentioned the possibility of canceling subsidies. After this news spread, elementary school teachers were extremely alarmed, resulting in a suicide by lying on the railway tracks. Zhu Qixiang, a native of this county, had been an elementary school teacher in a certain school in the district for many years, owing a considerable amount of back pay. Unable to obtain payment after repeated demands, Qixiang was forced to commit suicide out of anger. The day before yesterday, late at night, he secretly lay down on the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway bridge No. 36. Because it was dark, he was run over by the train wheels and died. It was not until this morning that a farmer going to the market discovered the incident. The farmer reported it to the local police. A crowd gathered and saw the deceased lying face down on the iron bridge, with his waist crushed by the wheels. The scene was extremely tragic.

Ningbo

World Bookstore Completely Burned Down

The World Bookstore on Cuiya Street in this port has been open for ten years. It has been managed by Zhi Xiaoyun, a native of Zhenhai. There are thirteen employees and apprentices in total. Because the store is small, there is a warehouse in Sha帽di. Employees sleep in the warehouse at night, and six apprentices sleep in the store. Four of them sleep in the store hall, and two sleep upstairs. The store does not usually have cooking fires. The employees all eat boxed lunches. Last night, around 10:30, a fire suddenly broke out in the books in the store hall. The ladder was soon burned down. When the apprentices Xu Dingwan and Wang Yifu heard the fire downstairs, they jumped out of the windows upstairs. In a short time, they were gone. Later, the various fire brigades arrived after hearing the alarm and put out the fire after about half an hour. In addition to the complete destruction of the bookstore, the overhanging building of the Changhe Foreign Goods Store to the left and the three-story single room of the China Rubber Raincoat Cloth Factory's retail department to the right were also affected, as well as the top of the three-story building of the Weiyuan General Goods Store. The estimated loss is over 20,000 yuan. The missing apprentice Xu Dingwan has not yet been found and is currently being searched for.

Xiaoshan

Careless Silk Reeling Causes Fire Spreading to Eleven Homes

Zhu Alan, a farmer in Shengdi Township, 6th district of Xiaoshan, because the spring cocoon prices raised this year have plummeted and the value is not enough to offset the leaf prices, was reeling fresh cocoons into silk on the night of the 30th. Unexpectedly, a fire was left unattended in the firewood overnight, which spread to the kitchen and quickly engulfed the sky with flames, making it impossible to approach. It then spread to ten neighboring homes, causing losses of over 30,000 yuan. Also, Zhu Alan's twelve-year-old daughter, who was sleeping soundly in the room when the fire broke out, did not have time to escape and was tragically burned to death.

Local News

National Products Movement Exhibition Opened Yesterday Representative of the Ministry of Industry He Bingxian Unveiled the Ceremony Mayor's Representative Zhang Yuanruo Raised the Flag

▲·········▲

Over Ten Thousand People Attended, Creating a Grand Occasion

The Shanghai National Products Movement Exhibition, sponsored by the China National Products Manufacturers Association, held its opening ceremony yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM. Representative of the Ministry of Industry He Bingxian unveiled the ceremony, and Mayor Wu's representative Zhang Yuanruo raised the flag. No fewer than ten thousand representatives from all walks of life and guests attended the ceremony. The ceremony was very grand. The speeches by the guests elaborated on the meaning of promoting national products in great detail. There was also entertainment to add to the excitement. The details are recorded below.

(A Glimpse of the Venue)

The exhibition venue is located between Xiaoximen, Penglai Road, and Yongning Road, covering an area of more than ten acres. Two large pine and cypress archways were built along the road, with the words "Production Saves the Country," "National Products Save the Country," and "Shanghai National Products Movement Exhibition" written on them. The couplets read "Concentrate national production, develop national spirit," "Do not let millions of dollars flow into foreign lands, remember the heavy national humiliation in your hearts," "Economic aggression is worse than military aggression, the national products movement is a salvation movement," "Come here and I guarantee you will be excited and inspired, and marvel at the sight," "From today onwards, whether it is clothing, food, housing, or transportation, use national products." The venue is full of exquisite national products displayed by various factories. Ladies from all walks of life were very enthusiastic to visit. In the center of the venue, there is a large auditorium with a portrait of Sun Yat-sen hanging in the middle, with the party and national flags crossed on both sides. The center of the stage is for the chairman and representatives from all walks of life, and the right is for the record seat. The layout is simple and neat. In front, there is a large advertising sign of Taikang Company, which is two zhang high and about ten zhang wide, which is especially eye-catching. Around the venue, the security team of the Public Security Bureau maintained order.

(Guest Signatures)

Guests who signed their names included Wang Xiaolai, Wang Yansong, He Bingxian, Chen Yiting, Zhang Yichen, Hu Xiyuan, Chen Jicheng, Lin Kecong, Chen Binghui, Zhang Yuanruo, Wu Yushu, Lin Kanghou, Chen Jiufeng, Chen Jingsheng, Zheng Dongshan, Fang Yalan, Yu Zhongxian, Xu Genghua, Wang Hanzhang, Sun Chucheng, Xu Letian, and others.

(Unveiling and Flag Raising)

At 2:00 PM, the music team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau played music to open the meeting. The members of the presidium Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Wu Zhihao, Wang Yansong, Yu Hualong, Zhang Yichen, Chen Jicheng, Chen Binghui, Liu Zhongying, Xue Fuji, Hu Xiyuan, Zhang Yuanruo, He Bingxian, and representatives from various party and government circles entered the venue in succession and circled to the main entrance of the assembly. The representative of the Ministry of Industry, He Bingxian, cut the ribbon at the main gate, and the whole audience burst into thunderous applause. The chairman then led Mayor Wu's representative, Zhang Yuanruo, to walk to the flagpole and held the flag-raising ceremony amid the melodious music.

(Chairman's Report)

After the chairman group finished the unveiling and flag-raising ceremony, they returned to the podium. Chairman Wang Yansong gave a brief report, saying, "Today is the day for the opening ceremony of the Shanghai National Products Movement Exhibition. Today, everyone knows that national products should be promoted. Therefore, national products movements have been held repeatedly. Although the results are slightly better than in previous years, there are still many areas where we need to continue to work hard. Looking at the customs report, in the midst of active resistance, inferior goods have been slightly affected. Up to now, inferior goods have become active again and will be sold to the Chinese market again, which is very worrying. I hope that in the future, national products manufacturers will strive to improve their products, and citizens should also enthusiastically purchase and use them, so that our national economy will not be completely invaded and the national lifeline will not be severely destroyed."

(Representative's Speech)

Next, He Bingxian, Director of the Bureau of International Trade and Representative of the Ministry of Industry, delivered a speech. He said, "Since our country has traded with various countries, the annual import surplus has always been between 700 million and 800 million yuan. Why is the import surplus so large and there are so many foreign goods? This is because our country itself cannot have a large production of national products. If there are few national products, we cannot have an export surplus and cannot find markets abroad. National products merchants should be alert in the future and not be obsessed with making profits. If they see that someone is making a profit with a certain product, they will rush to it. They should create their own and not compete with each other. Also, business should not be expected to make a ten thousandfold profit, because this is impossible in economics. It is okay to invest money in business, but speculation is absolutely not allowed. This is the humble opinion I offer at the meeting today." Next, Zhang Yuanruo, the representative of the municipal government, gave a speech, saying, "Why are Chinese people poor and Europeans and Americans rich? It is because Chinese people want to send money to foreigners. In the future, to carry out the national products movement, all Chinese people must work hard and not send money to foreigners. Looking at the German man Haijing Bo, who came to Shanghai last year to do circus performances, he brought everything, no matter how small, from Germany. The Germans were unwilling to give a penny to our people. This kind of spirit is worth emulating. Diligence and hard work are essential to promoting national products." Next, Wang Xiaolai, the representative of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, gave a speech, saying, "Promoting national products is useless to talk empty words. We must make up our minds to find a way out. First, do not buy things (Western goods), and second, do not spend useless money, such as cigarettes, which should not be consumed at all, because this thing is completely burned to ashes, and the raw materials are all foreign goods." Finally, Lin Kecong, the representative of the Women's National Products Year Movement Committee, Chen Jingsheng, the representative of the Bureau of International Trade, Chen Yiting, Chen Jicheng, Tao Leqin, Yu Zhongxian, Cao Zhigong, and others gave speeches. The full text is omitted.

(Tour of the Assembly)

Inside the venue, more than 600 temporary sheds were built. The arrangements of each factory were colorful and had everything. The Huatong Electrical Manufacturing Factory and Taikang Food Company were the most eye-catching. The whole venue had more than ten planned routes, including Salvation Road, National Products Road, Northeast Road, Production Road, Industry Road, Fengtian Road, Jilin Road, Heilongjiang Road, Rehe Road, Manufacturer Road, People's Livelihood Road, and New Life Road. The streets were clean and orderly.

Radio Broadcast

After the opening ceremony of the assembly, the presidium Chen Binghui and others went to the radio station to broadcast, with the themes "The National Products Movement is a Salvation Movement," "Only Hard Work in Production Can Save Us from Danger," and "National Products are an Iron Army to Resist Aggression," which ended around 5:00 PM.

Entertainment

In order to increase the audience's interest, the association hired members of the Gujin Troupe to perform entertainment, with the programs "From Now on Prosperity," "Du Shiniang," and singing and dancing. More than 50 members of the troupe performed on stage, and the audience was very enthusiastic.

The May Festival Passed Safely, Guard Was Lifted Yesterday, Tomorrow is the Communist Party Memorial, So Temporary Precautions Are Still Necessary

The eventful May Festival has passed safely. The Municipal Public Security Bureau lifted the all-day alert yesterday. However, tomorrow is the Communist Party Memorial Day, so it ordered the subordinates to intensify precautions according to the usual alert methods. The details are recorded below.

Guard Lifted Yesterday

In order to maintain local security during the May Revolution Memorial Festival, the Municipal Public Security Bureau ordered all districts to implement alerts and decided on joint defense measures with the Songhu Garrison Command, the Security Office, and other agencies to cooperate. From the May 1st Labor Day to the May 30th Nanjing Road Massacre Memorial Day, the entire month was under intensified prevention. Fortunately, no disturbances occurred. Now that the May Festival has passed, Wen Hongen, Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, will lift the all-month alert order from yesterday and encourage the heads of the various districts to work hard to defend the local area. In the future, on memorial days, the usual precautions will be taken.

Temporary Precautions Tomorrow

Tomorrow (June 3rd) is the memorial day for the establishment of the Communist Party's Shanghai Federation of Industry, Commerce and Students. The authorities of the Chinese Concession Police reported that the Communist Party will hold a demonstration on that day, which will likely cause disturbances. Therefore, a temporary alert was announced for one day. Wen Hongen, Director of the Public Security Bureau, ordered all districts under his command to dispatch additional officers to patrol and inspectors and detectives to lead plainclothes inspectors to check pedestrians at the border of the Chinese Concession to maintain peace within the boundary.

Gengkuan British Gold Bonds Underwritten by Four Chinese and Foreign Banks Decision to Issue Subscription Vouchers First

Xin Sheng News reported that the 6% British Gold Gengkuan Bonds of 1.5 million pounds of the 23rd year of the Republic of China were issued yesterday and were underwritten by the four banks, the Central, China, Communications, and HSBC. The contract is about to be signed, and it was decided to issue subscription vouchers first. The details are recorded below.

Signing the Contract The Ministry of Railways, in order to complete the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, used the Gengkuan as collateral and, together with the Ministry of Finance, issued the 6% British Gold Gengkuan Bonds of the 23rd year of the Republic of China yesterday, which was underwritten by the four banks, the Central, China, Communications, and HSBC. It was stipulated that it would be issued at 96% of the face value. However, the underwriting of the four banks was slightly lower than the 96% issuance. The Ministry of Finance has negotiated with the four banks, HSBC, etc., and the underwriting is appropriate. The contract has been drafted and can be officially signed in the coming days.

Issuing Subscription Vouchers A reporter from Xin Sheng News learned from the banking industry yesterday that after these bonds are underwritten by the four banks, the Central Bank, etc., the four banks will promote them to domestic banks. If domestic banks and domestic banks want to purchase these bonds, they will be managed by the four underwriting banks. As for these bonds, they have not yet been printed. The Ministry of Finance has decided to issue subscription vouchers first and then exchange them after the bonds are printed. Although the subscription vouchers can be freely bought, sold, and mortgaged, they cannot circulate in the bond market.

A Nanjing telegram from the Central News Agency on the 1st stated that a total of 1.5 million pounds of 6% British Gold Gengkuan Bonds of the 23rd year of the Republic of China were issued on the 1st. It is stipulated that the first principal will be repaid on January 1st next year, and the principal and interest will be fully repaid by January 1st of the 36th year. These bonds will be used as a construction fund to complete the Guangdong-Hankou Railway and were issued on the 1st.

The Face Value of the Italian Gengkuan Loan Certificate Has Been Agreed Upon with the Banking Group by the Ministry of Finance

Each Bank Will Issue Four Certificates of Principal and Interest Per Month

The Banking Group is Allowed to Mortgage to the Central Bank and the Preparatory Committee

The Ministry of Finance will use the Gengkuan returned by Italy as collateral to borrow 44 million yuan from 16 banks including the Central Bank. The loans have long been paid in full by the various borrowing banks. The face value of the loan certificates has been agreed upon with the banking group organized by the 16 banks including the Central Bank and the Ministry of Finance and can be mortgaged to the Central Bank and the Shanghai Bankers Association Joint Preparatory Committee at any time for circulation in the market. As for the rumor from the Beijing telegram yesterday that the Ministry of Finance issued 30 million yuan in securities, it is not accurate. The details learned by the reporter from Xin Xin News are recorded as follows.

Repaying Principal and Interest According to the loan contract, the certificates that the Ministry of Finance should issue to the banking group, the certificates from January to June of the 23rd year of the Republic of China, have been handed over to the banking group by the Ministry of Finance at the end of April and transferred to the various borrowing banks. As for the principal and interest due at the end of May, it was paid by the Customs to the Central Bank on the 31st, and the Central Bank transferred it to the banking group, and then the banking group distributed it to the various borrowing banks separately, which was paid in full.

Face Value of the Certificate The number of certificates has been agreed upon by both the Ministry of Finance and the banking group. The method is that each bank will issue two certificates of principal and interest each month, one of which is an integer and the other is a zero. For example, if a bank borrows 35,600 yuan, 30,000 yuan will be written on one certificate, and 5,600 yuan will be written on another certificate. The other two certificates will write the interest amount of integers and zeros. It is also heard that the certificates have been commissioned by the National Treasury Department of the Ministry of Finance to be printed by the Shanghai China Bookstore and will be implemented from July this year.

Permission to Mortgage According to the loan contract, the banking group is originally allowed to issue 30 million yuan of securities at one time. After the Ministry of Finance negotiated with the banking group, the Ministry of Finance issued certificates for mutual mortgage, and the issuance of 30 million yuan of securities was suspended. According to a reporter from Xin Xin News, who learned from the banking group, in order to regulate finance, the Ministry of Finance, in addition to stipulating that the certificates can be mortgaged to the banking group banks, has now also allowed them to be mortgaged to the Central Bank and the Shanghai Bankers Association Joint Preparatory Committee at any time for circulation in the market.

Beijing Telegram Misreported Yesterday, a Beijing telegram said that the Ministry of Finance had obtained the consent of the banking group to change the previous 30 million yuan of securities to be issued by the Ministry of Finance, and the losses suffered by the banking group would be recognized and subsidized by the Ministry of Finance. Yesterday, a reporter from Xin Xin News specially inquired about this from various aspects of the banking industry and the banking group in this city. The rumor is completely inaccurate and is impossible in fact. The Italian Gengkuan has been borrowed by the Ministry of Finance from the banking group, and the cash has been used. If another 30 million yuan of securities is issued, it is the same collateral used for two different mortgages. Not only will the banking group be unable to agree, but the Ministry of Finance may not have this opinion. Moreover, the Ministry of Finance has now designated certificates that can be mortgaged to each other at any time, so there is no need to issue securities again.

The Central Gengkuan [Boxer Indemnity Funds] Board of Directors Approves Distribution Amounts

The Board of Directors for the management of the British Boxer Indemnity Funds, since its establishment, has been in operation for over three years. In accordance with the resolutions of the Central Political Conference and the exchange of notes between China and Britain, the Gengkuan funds under the Board's management must first be used as a fund for the reorganization of railways and other productive enterprises, and then the 5% interest income from the loans will be used to subsidize educational and cultural undertakings. Currently, the total amount of subsidies up to the end of June this year is 1,337,589 yuan. The Education Group of the Board held a three-day meeting last month to thoroughly examine all applications for funds from various educational and cultural institutions since its establishment. It was decided to allocate 1.2 million yuan in whole numbers according to the interest income distribution standards and proportions approved by the Executive Yuan for record, and to subsidize separately. The remaining amount of more than 130,000 yuan will be used as a special reserve fund for special education projects. The 24th plenary meeting of the Board of Directors reviewed the examination report in detail and unanimously approved the distribution amounts as follows: Four categories: 1. National Central Museum, 2. National Central Library. Each of the above two museums will be subsidized with a construction fee of 1.5 million yuan, with 150,000 yuan allocated to each this year. Category B: 1. The Board of Directors will establish six professorships, each with an annual responsibility of 10,000 yuan, limited to three years, and will be awarded to Central University, Sun Yat-sen University, Wuhan University, Zhejiang University, Peiyang Engineering College, and the Central Health Laboratory, one each. 2. National Central Research Institute, to subsidize the manufacturing of scientific instruments and equipment with 100,000 yuan, to be allocated in three years, with 30,000 yuan each for the first and second years, and 40,000 yuan for the third year. 3. National Peiping Research Institute to subsidize equipment expenses of 100,000 yuan, with 60,000 yuan to subsidize the Physics Research Institute and 40,000 yuan to subsidize the Chemistry Research Institute, to be allocated in three years, with 30,000 yuan each for the first and second years, and 40,000 yuan for the third year. 4. National Central University, one professorship awarded (see first case). 5. National Sun Yat-sen University, one professorship awarded (see first case), and a subsidy of 110,000 yuan for equipment expenses, to be allocated equally in three years. 6. National Wuhan University, one professorship awarded (see first case), and a subsidy of 120,000 yuan for the construction of the Engineering College, to be allocated equally in three years. 7. National Zhejiang University, one professorship awarded (see first case), and a subsidy of 120,000 yuan for equipment expenses, to be allocated equally in three years, with 50,000 yuan to subsidize the Agricultural College, 35,000 yuan to subsidize the Engineering College, and 35,000 yuan to subsidize the Physics Department of the Science College. 8. Private Nankai University, to subsidize the equipment expenses of the Mathematics Department with 20,000 yuan per year, limited to three years. 9. Private Yenching University, to subsidize equipment expenses of 45,000 yuan, to be allocated equally in three years. 10. Private Xiamen University, to subsidize the purchase of scientific books with 30,000 yuan, to be allocated equally in three years. 11. National Peiyang Engineering College, one professorship awarded (see first case). 12. National Shanghai Medical College, to subsidize construction expenses of 60,000 yuan, to be allocated equally in three years. 13. Hunan-Yale Medical College, a provincial institution, to subsidize equipment expenses of 60,000 yuan, to be allocated equally in three years. 14. The Scottish Church of the Three Eastern Provinces, Liaoning Medical College, to subsidize

equipment expenses of 20,000 yuan. 15. Central Hygiene Laboratory, one professorship awarded (see first case), and a subsidy of 60,000 yuan for equipment expenses, to be allocated equally in three years. 16. National Translation and Compilation Bureau, to subsidize construction expenses of 50,000 yuan, to be allocated equally in two years. 17. China-British Cultural Association, to subsidize construction expenses of 20,000 yuan. 18. China Architectural Society, to subsidize the compilation of illustrated books with 20,000 yuan, to be allocated equally in two years. Category C: Scholarship expenses of 180,000 yuan. Nine students have already been sent to the UK last year, and it is planned to send another 31 this year. All required public expenses and examination expenses will be paid from this 180,000 yuan. Category D: 1. Prize money of 4,000 yuan for soliciting advanced elementary school history textbooks. 2. Prize money of 4,000 yuan for soliciting elementary school music songs. 3. Prize money of 4,000 yuan for soliciting textbooks for popular education. Category E: 1. Special rural education expenses for the Jiangxi recovered bandit area, a subsidy of 400,000 yuan, and in accordance with the provisions of the interest income distribution standards and proportions, limited to four years (this year, in addition to the 137,589 yuan borrowed from the special reserve fund, the remaining 262,411 yuan will be made up from this category). 2. A subsidy of 12,000 yuan to Ningxia Province to build an elementary school. 3. A subsidy of 12,000 yuan to Qinghai Province to build an elementary school (the interest income allocated to Category E, totaling 288,000 yuan, in addition to subsidizing the above three cases, there is a remaining balance of 1,589 yuan, which will be rolled into the reserve fund). The above categories distribute 1.2 million yuan, plus 137,589 yuan borrowed from the special reserve fund, totaling 1,336,000 yuan. According to the person in charge of the Board, from the start of the formal review of cases to the present, there have been a total of 121 cases, with the total amount of requested funds reaching more than 56 million yuan, which is far different from the amount of interest income received, making the distribution even more difficult. Therefore, based on the previously established distribution standards, and after repeated deliberation, the current urgent needs of domestic educational and cultural undertakings were used as the basis for the review, to provide relatively favorable subsidies: (1) The capital is the focus of attention from all sides and should also be the cultural center of the country, so the construction of the two Central Museums and Libraries should be based on the established cases when the Board was first established, and make every effort to assist in promoting their establishment. (2) After the Jiangxi bandit area was recovered, the economy collapsed, and people's livelihood was devastated. Recruiting the displaced people is precisely to curb the emergence of chaos and to handle the aftermath. The need for funds is particularly urgent, so subsidies should be given for the special rural education in the recovered bandit area to facilitate its implementation. (3) The current applications for funds are mostly from higher education institutions. Since it is impossible to distribute them universally, we can only follow the previously established distribution standards and give priority to the four disciplines of agriculture, engineering, medicine, and science, and to those who have submitted relatively concrete plans, and provide as much assistance as possible. For those who request fees in more than two types, we will consider the situation and select the essentials for assistance. For example, those who subsidize construction fees will no longer subsidize equipment fees, and those who subsidize equipment fees will no longer subsidize construction fees. (4) In order to promote the development of culture and education in remote provinces, even if there are no requests that fully meet the standards and concrete plans, special subsidies will be given within the possible scope. (5) According to the resolution of the 16th meeting of the Board of Directors, 20 students should be sent to the UK every year. In addition to the nine students who have already been sent last year, it is planned to send another 30 students this year, plus the vacancy of 11 from last year, for a total of 31. Therefore, this scholarship fund should be reserved first for application.

The Electrical Short-Term and Long-Term Public Bonds Were Drawn Yesterday Morning to Redeem Principal, Totaling Over 313,000 Yuan in Principal and Interest. Payment Will Be Made by the Central and Other Three Banks at the End of This Month.

The seventh redemption drawing of the Electrical Enterprise Short-Term and Long-Term Public Bonds issued by the National Government Construction Committee was held at the Bankers' Association yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. A total of ten lots were drawn, and the principal and interest to be redeemed totaled 313,550 yuan. The winning numbers are scheduled to be paid by the Central, China, and Communications Banks in Shanghai and Nanjing at the end of this month.

Representatives Present

Those present included Liu Baixin, Secretary-General of the Construction Committee; Chen Zhaolin, Director of the Purchasing Committee; Yang Zhaiwang, Wang Fangsheng, and Zhou Yingpei, members of the Electrical Enterprise Long-Term and Short-Term Public Bond Custody Committee; Song Boxuan of the Ministry of Finance; Wang Gengtang of the Auditing Department; Lu Wenshao of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce; Lin Kanghou of the Bankers' Association; Zhang Mengzhou of the Money Dealers' Association; Fan Jietang of the National Debt Fund Custody Committee; Jin Wenyuan of the Central Bank; Yang Dunfu of the Shanghai Bank; Mao Rui of the Communications Bank; Han Diaoqing of the Bank of China; Qu Jigang of the Guohua Bank; Xu Gongquan of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank; and Ebbes of Siemens and others, totaling more than 30 people.

Chairman's Report

After performing the ceremony, Chairman Liu Baixin reported, saying that today is the seventh redemption drawing of the Electrical Enterprise Short-Term and Long-Term Public Bonds of the National Government Construction Committee. It is an honor to have all sectors attend and supervise. The issued amount of short-term public bonds is 2.5 million, and the principal has been redeemed six times, totaling 1.05 million. The unredeemed principal is 1.45 million. This drawing includes seven lots, and the principal to be redeemed is 175,000 yuan, so the remaining amount is 1.275 million. The interest paid this time is 58,000 yuan. The issued amount of electrical enterprise long-term public bonds is 1.5 million, and the principal has been redeemed six times, totaling 315,000 yuan. The unredeemed principal is 1.185 million. This drawing includes three lots, and the principal to be redeemed is 45,000 yuan, so the remaining amount is 1.1 million. The interest paid this time is 35,550 yuan. The total of the above long and short-term seven redemptions is 220,000 yuan, plus the ninth interest payment of 93,550 yuan, totaling 313,550 yuan in principal and interest. Please check the lots and the lot register for verification before proceeding with the drawing.

Winning Numbers

After the chairman's report, the supervisors inspected

the lots and the lot register. Then, the drawers proceeded with the drawing. (1) Seven short-term lots were drawn, and the winning numbers are 20, 25, 47, 59, 62, 73, and 83. (2) Three long-term lots were drawn, and the winning numbers are 36, 48, and 76. Each lot drawn was sent to the chairman and supervisors for inspection and then entered into the register and announced on a placard. All winning numbers are scheduled to be paid by the Shanghai, Nanjing Central China Communications and other three banks starting at the end of this month.

Ma Yinchu Discusses Banning Prize Savings

Encouraging Luck Hinders Proper Savings

Capital Flows Out of the Interior, Causing Rural Hardship

Treaties Offer No Basis, Prohibition Should Not Be Hesitated

Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Ma Yinchu, Chairman of the Finance Committee of the Legislative Yuan, is highly regarded in China's financial and economic circles. At the National Financial Conference, he proposed to strictly prohibit the Sino-French and International Savings Societies and drafted (1) restrictions on future membership, (2) thorough investigation of the funds of both societies. After deliberation, it was decided to hand over the matter to the Ministry of Finance for verification. Ma Gong also believes that this kind of prize savings is extremely harmful to the national economy and people's livelihood, and for the purpose of making the people understand the inside story, he specially explained to the reporter of the Xin Sheng Beijing News the five greatest reasons for banning them and his personal feelings. The recorded comments are as follows:

Financial Conference

This National Financial Conference is the first grand financial meeting since the establishment of the National Government, and its significance is profound. When our country implements a controlled economy in the future, financial control must also be implemented at the same time. This Financial Conference is no less than the initial step in implementing controlled finance. Its purpose is to reduce the additional burdens of field taxes, abolish exorbitant taxes and miscellaneous levies, which can directly reduce the burden on farmers and indirectly promote production. It is an indispensable step for rescuing the rural economy today.

Rescuing the Countryside

Minister Kong also fully accommodated the proposals of this conference. The existing central stamp tax is not small, and at a time when finances are tight and all resources are exhausted, he was willing to resolutely allocate it for local application. His sincerity is evident. However, the aforementioned purpose of promoting production is complex and cannot be achieved simply by reducing the burden on farmers. What farmers lack is especially working capital. Therefore, rescuing the countryside and promoting production should especially involve lending low-interest, long-term funds to farmers. Farmers who are on the verge of death have hope of revival, and the purpose of promoting production can also be achieved. Currently, whether it is the academic community, the banking community, or people in political circles, they all unanimously call for the flow of funds from cities into the interior. Therefore, it can be said that their thinking is completely consistent.

Investing in the Interior

In fact, the banking community has invested a lot in the interior, such as railway investment, motor vehicle road investment, industrial investment, and electrical enterprise investment, which can be seen everywhere. Various banks have also established offices in the interior to directly lend funds to farmers, promote credit cooperatives, and buy and sell inland forward bills, all of which are aimed at realizing the hopes of all parties and have achieved excellent results. Since the financial community has taken such measures, the government authorities should also adopt a consistent policy, so that efforts can be concentrated and

things can be easily accomplished. Even in terms of savings funds, it should be the same, so that it can be invested in the interior as much as possible, which will benefit the rural economy.

Many Evils of Prize Money

However, today's prize savings is not the case. Not only can it not make savings funds flow into the interior, but the result is the opposite. It will cause funds from the interior to flow to the cities. Because the hard work of thrifty men and women in the interior is not enough to guarantee their lives, they all have a fluke mentality and try to seek improper gains, competing in speculation. The rural economy becomes more bankrupt, and their fluke mentality becomes even worse. The danger is very great. Prize savings is the most encouraging of fluke mentality, does not encourage thrift at all, and runs counter to the New Life Movement, which is being vigorously promoted. This is the first reason why it should be banned. The funds of prize savings not only flow from the countryside to the cities, contrary to our hopes, but also fear that most of them will flow overseas, causing harm to our country's industrialists. This is the second reason why it should be banned. Xu, Director of the Currency Department of the Ministry of Finance, has made every effort to promote thrift among the people in his proposal for compulsory savings at the conference. For prize savings that pretend to encourage thrift but actually collect money, he should strictly prohibit it. This is the third reason.

Should Be More Strict

Now the central government has strictly prohibited various banks from running prize savings. Chinese and foreign companies should be treated equally. Why is one side already implementing it, while the other side is allowed to exist? Moreover, the establishment of this kind of foreign prize savings institution has no treaty basis, but we are timid and dare not ban it, which is very puzzling. The prize savings

funds of the Sino-French Savings Society and the International Savings Society have reached nearly

90 million, of which the International Savings Society has more than 60 million and the Sino-French Savings Society has 20-30 million. The rate of increase is quite fast. If this continues, in the future, it will reach hundreds of millions, and its power will become increasingly strong and its supernatural powers will be vast. Our government will have the danger of not being able to control it, because the temptation will be greater and it will be more difficult to deal with. Therefore, for this kind of prize savings, we now hope that the government authorities with morality will quickly find a way to ban it. This is the fourth reason. Moreover, after the prevalence of prize savings, genuine savings are not easy to develop, because the financial resources of the people are limited. If they are abundant in this, they must be stingy in that. Therefore, if you want the genuine savings business to develop, you must prohibit prize savings. Now, the two prize savings societies not only set up shops in commercial ports to operate, but also set up offices in the interior. Local governments should also strictly prohibit them. This is the fifth reason.

Hard to Hesitate Again

In short, the prohibition of prize savings is a major matter, and the people from four aspects must work together to achieve the hope of reaching the goal: (1) Legislative aspect, (2) Party headquarters aspect, (4) Public opinion aspect. Newspapers are representatives of public opinion. Now the legislative public opinion Party headquarters and other parties are of course standing in opposition. We should combine and urge the administrative aspects to carry out the work in a practical manner. When savings funds only reached 20-30 million in the past, I already cried out loudly and strongly opposed it, but the financial authorities insisted on long-term research and delayed it. Now it has reached 60-70 million, and the financial authorities still have not changed their old habit of long-term research. I don't know when the research will have results. The situation is really something that outsiders cannot know. In my personal opinion, there is really no room for hesitation. I hope that the academic community and domestic scholars, Party headquarters and legislative aspects, will work together and unanimously advocate that the administrative side proceed as soon as possible to avoid being accused of regret and benefiting the rural economy.
