Sino-Japanese Radio Telegraph Put into Operation Yesterday; Four Japanese Type-Punching Machines Added; Heavy Traffic Yesterday.

The Sino-Japanese radio telegraph, which was being prepared by the International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, was put into operation at zero hours yesterday morning. There was a lot of traffic between the two sides. The Chinese headquarters is in Zhenru, while the Japanese headquarters is in Tokyo. Therefore, all telegrams sent from Shanghai to Japan are forwarded by the Tokyo headquarters to the recipients. Telegrams sent from Japan to China are forwarded by the Shanghai headquarters. The procedure is still convenient.

Additional Purchase of Japanese Machines

This Sino-Japanese communication uses the Chinese, English, and Japanese languages. Type-punching machines for the Chinese and English languages have been purchased by the radio stations. However, type-punching machines for the Japanese language are still missing. Therefore, the station had to purchase additional equipment from Japan for application. There are four of these machines, which were brought to Shanghai on the 30th of last month by engineers Hirako Taro, Shinhuri Masayoshi, and Shimada Shinjiro from the Tokyo Radio Station of Japan. They visited Engineer Zhang of the International Radio Station to hand over the machines for application.

Charging Method

The telegram fee from Shanghai to Japan is 75 centimes per word. According to the current market price,

one franc is equal to one yuan in Chinese currency, which is 7.5 jiao per word. For Chinese and Japanese telegrams, the fee is charged according to the number of words. According to the regulations of the station, (1) the name, address, place of delivery, and name and address of the recipient, regardless of the number of words, are all counted as one word. However, for copied telegrams, an additional word should be charged for each additional recipient name and address. (2) For Chinese telegrams, numbers can be used to write continuously, such as the two characters "Zhong Hua" can be written as "○○二二五四七

八." Every seven numbers are counted as one word, which is more than three times cheaper than the original method of calculating fees for foreign language telegrams. For Japanese telegrams, Japanese kana must be used to write, and every seven kana are counted as one word. The International Cloud Terrace in Sassoon House on Nanjing Road also has detailed methods for inquiries from all walks of life.

Jing'an Steamer Lawsuit

The Court Ordered a Guarantee of 80,000 Yuan, Not Compensation; the Company Has Not Acknowledged It and Has Petitioned the Government for Review.

Mr. Yu Qiaqing, General Manager of Sanbei Steamer Wharf Co., Ltd., sent a letter to this newspaper yesterday, saying that he had read in today's newspaper that the company's Jing'an steamer had lost the lawsuit and the court had ruled to pay 80,000 yuan in compensation. This is inconsistent with the facts. The court ordered the company to provide a guarantee of 80,000 yuan in valuable securities. The company believes that the court failed to deal with the matter in accordance with maritime conditions, and the plaintiff was actually guilty of false accusation. Failure to order a guarantee sets a bad precedent that is relevant to the national shipping industry and cannot be approved. It has already petitioned the government for review. The report in your newspaper has a relationship with the company's reputation and business. The corresponding letter is for investigation and correction. The Shanghai Local Court's criminal instruction of May 29 is appended below: Yu Qiaqing's request for the return of the Jing'an steamer is known. Since the company claims that the Jing'an steamer belongs to the company and the company is responsible for fulfilling the judgment in the future, immediately issue a certificate and submit it to the court for verification so that it can be released. Panchen Lama's Lecture at Jinan University Yesterday

State Council Member Panchen Lama, since arriving in Shanghai from Hangzhou, has been quite busy visiting various factories and schools these past few days. Yesterday afternoon at 4 p.m., he accepted the invitation of Jinan University President Shen Pengfei to deliver a lecture at the university. Accompanied by Section Chief Li Dachao of the Municipal Government, he first rested in the President's office for a moment before proceeding to the auditorium, where faculty and students greeted him with applause. The Lama walked to the podium, where President Shen Pengfei introduced him. The Lama then began his lecture, (translated by Wang Dejun), saying, "Gentlemen, students, I am honored to be invited by your President to visit and give a lecture. I don't have much to say, but recalling my departure from Tibet more than a decade ago, I have witnessed the year-by-year progress of domestic politics, which I find most gratifying. This credit, of course, goes to the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. We know that the Premier's doctrine is one of national salvation, and I hope it will be realized soon. I also hope that you, the students, will work hard to promote its realization, because schools are of great importance. A country's schools are a key element, and if schools perform well, the country will naturally be saved. The Premier's works have also expressed the hope that everyone will strive to alleviate human suffering in the future and seek national equality. As for myself, I have gained a lot of experience in the mainland over the past decade, and recently, I will use what I have learned, following the instructions of the central government, to resolve the disputes between Kang and Tibet and restore China's original glory. I also hope that everyone will provide assistance. Finally, I hope that if Tibetan students come to the mainland to study in the future, perhaps they will come to your school, and I hope you will guide them." After the lecture, he visited the library and physics and chemistry laboratories, and then took a car to the Wuqian Radio Station for a visit.

Minutes of the 168th Joint Meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees of the Lawyers Association

The Shanghai Lawyers Association convened its 168th joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees at its meeting place at the intersection of Avenue Petain and Rue Lafayette in the French Concession at 7 p.m. the night before. The committee members present were Wu Zhengjue, Zhou Xiao'an, Chen Zhigao, Li Ming, Shen Junru, Yang Zhihao, Mao Yun, Zhu Fuqiu, Wu Kaisheng, Wang Weizhen, Chen Tingrui, and others. Chen Tingrui was publicly elected as chairman, and Dai Jixian served as recorder. The meeting proceeded as scheduled. The motions discussed are recorded below: (1) The Lawyers Association sent a letter informing that the Ministry had approved the organization of a Legal Aid Society for the Poor by various member associations. (Resolution) To organize a Legal Aid Society for the Poor, solicit the participation of various members. The rules and regulations for the operation of the society shall be drafted by the Standing Committee and submitted to the Executive and Supervisory Committees for approval. (2) The Shanghai Second Special District Local Court sent a letter informing that cases heard by the Civil Division should comply with the time specified in the summons and report to the court. (Resolution) To inform all members and reply to the court. (3) The Shanghai Second Special District Local Court scheduled the burning of opium and smoking paraphernalia and requested the dispatch of personnel to supervise. (Resolution) To nominate Committee Member Wu Kaisheng to supervise. (4) The Jiangsu First District Tobacco and Alcohol Tax and License Tax Collection Bureau inquired whether Zhou Xianjue had ever practiced as a lawyer and whether his address could be investigated and replied to. (Resolution) To investigate and reply. (5) Member Song Yunhui sent a letter reporting that permission had been granted. (Resolution) To grant permission. (6) Member Zhou Yu proposed that the Shanghai Local Court should not follow the practice of the Shanghai First and Second Special Districts in designating pro bono defense lawyers by rotating among the members of the association, and requested that the matter be discussed and implemented uniformly. (Resolution) To investigate the method of designating pro bono defense lawyers, which is the authority of the court and not suitable for discussion. (7) Whether members whose addresses are unknown and who owe excessive membership fees, and members who simply owe excessive fees and have repeatedly failed to pay despite reminders, should be reported for withdrawal from the association according to the regulations. (Resolution) To report for withdrawal from the association according to the regulations. (8) Yang Bingxun sent a letter reporting that lawyer Zhu Zhishan, representing a client, published an advertisement containing insulting language, and requested that disciplinary action be considered. (Resolution) The content of the advertisement published by Lawyer Zhu on behalf of his client does not contain any insulting content. As for the leaflet, since no lawyer is named, it cannot be considered to damage reputation. The reporter should be informed accordingly. (9) Committee Member Wu Kaisheng proposed that in the unfortunate event of a dispute between a client and a member or between members, both parties should first attempt reconciliation or report to the association for mediation, and should not directly file a lawsuit in court to maintain discipline. (Resolution) Regarding the second point of the proposal, to forward a letter to all members for attention. (10) (Omitted) (11) Lawyer Tang Zhixian applied for membership. (Resolution) Approved. The meeting adjourned late at night.

Xie Zhongle Fills Vacancy on Chamber of Commerce Executive Committee Due to Xiang Songmao's Death

Following Xiang Songmao's death during the January 28th Incident, his remains were not recovered and his family did not make a declaration, and the General Principles of the Civil Code stipulate that a missing person can only be considered dead after three years of disappearance and a declaration. Therefore, the vacancy has not been filled. Now, since his family has held a funeral, but the formality of a declaration of death is still lacking, the Chamber of Commerce submitted a request to the Bureau of Social Affairs for instructions on whether to fill the vacancy. On the 30th of this month, the Chamber of Commerce received approval No. 3996 from the Bureau of Social Affairs, which stated, "The matter has been noted. Since Xiang Songmao, an Executive Committee member of the Chamber of Commerce, has been deceased for a long time and his position is vacant, the vacant Executive Committee position should be filled by the alternate committee members in order of precedence. Please be informed accordingly." Upon receiving this approval, the order of the alternate Executive Committee members was checked, and it was determined that the vacancy should be filled by Xie Zhongle. Mr. Xie has already been notified to fill the vacancy.

Demolition of Sunken Ships between Anqing and Jiujiang Announced by Hydrographic Office

The Hydrographic Office issued a notice to shipping vessels yesterday, announcing that the demolition of sunken ships near the Anqing-Jiujiang section of the Yangtze River has been partially completed and that beacon lights have been removed. The notice urged the shipping community to pay attention to the location of the demolition of sunken ships at 307 degrees north from the Zhenjiang Tower, at a distance of 57 chains (every ten chains equals one nautical mile), approximately 116 degrees 1 minute East longitude and 29 degrees 45 minutes North latitude. The depth of the partially demolished area is 5 feet (1.52 meters) at the Jiujiang water level zero point.

Water Cut-Off Dispute in Peide Lane Resolved Yesterday: Water Installed by Tenants, Rent Reduced by Two Yuan Per Month

According to the Huadong News Agency, the water cut-off dispute in Peide Lane on Xinzha Road, which lasted for more than a month, has been resolved satisfactorily. Taikoo's New "Shuntien" Vessel Hosts Reception for All Circles; Maiden Voyage to North China Today

To improve its regular North China line vessels, Taikoo Dockyard in Hong Kong built the new "Shuntien" vessel to replace the old "Shuntien" on the Shanghai, Qingdao, Yantai, Weihaiwei, Tianjin, and other routes. The vessel is the newest and fastest of the seagoing vessels, with passenger accommodations divided into first, second, third, and steerage classes. Yesterday, the company hosted a reception for guests from all walks of life to tour the vessel, as described below:

Elegant Design: The new "Shuntien" vessel has a carrying capacity of 3,000 tons, and its construction is the latest in seagoing vessels. The interior equipment is all in the style of foreign ocean liners. The lifeboats on the deck are suspended from external supports, providing space for passengers to stroll. The arrangement of the first and second class cabins is even better than the new "Shengjing," and the vessel travels smoothly. The journey from Shanghai to Qingdao takes only 24 hours, making it the best and fastest vessel on the Shanghai-North China route.

Reception and Tour: The new "Shuntien" vessel was docked at the company's wharf in the French Concession. Yesterday, Taikoo's Shipping Manager Bai Lihua, Chinese Manager Yang Meinan, Shipping Manager Yang Shaonan, and employees Zhang Zhipan, Zhang Dongge, Xu Youren, along with the vessel's comprador Sun Yangshan and Changcheng Firm Manager Shen Guohua, hosted guests. From 11 a.m. to 12 p.m., foreign reporters, British consuls, and other foreign guests were invited to tour the vessel. From 4 p.m. to 6 p.m., customs brokers and Chinese guests were invited, including Shi Zhikun, Chairman of the Customs Brokers Association, Yu Qiaqing, and more than 100 other people. All praised the vessel's excellence.

Maiden Voyage Today: The new "Shuntien" vessel is scheduled to depart from Shanghai on its maiden voyage to North China today, after which it will regularly run the route. The company will redeploy the original "Shuntien" vessel to run the direct route from the Yangtze River to Southeast Asia. Many passengers are embarking on the new "Shuntien" today, with first-class cabins available in both single and double configurations, making it very complete.

"Gongping" Vessel Importing Goods Yesterday Damaged Cargo Ship at Dock Due to Broken Cable While Turning, Cargo Ship Carrying Matchsticks Hit

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Gongping" vessel, which arrived in Shanghai yesterday carrying goods from Qingdao, broke a mooring cable while entering the port and crashed into a cargo barge, causing significant losses. The details are as follows:

Cable Breaks, Vessel Crashes

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's "Gongping" vessel, which arrived in Shanghai from Qingdao yesterday, entered the port around 3 p.m. When the vessel reached the Jinliyuan dock on the South Bund, it was preparing to moor alongside the riverbank. The "Gongping" first used a steel cable to secure to the riverbank, then began to turn to moor. Unexpectedly, the tide was high and the current was strong, and the steel cable suddenly snapped. The "Gongping" vessel's hull suddenly leaned sharply towards the dock, and there was a cargo barge moored next to the dock, which was unable to avoid the collision and was destroyed.

Cargo Ship Damaged

A cargo barge belonging to Jinhongsheng, which was transporting 100 bundles of matchsticks from the Huachang Match Factory in Zhangjiabang, Pudong to the China Merchants' "Tonghua" vessel for shipment to Shantou, was in the process of customs inspection when the "Gongping" vessel's broken cable caused it to swing in and collide with the barge. The cargo ship was unable to avoid the collision, and its stern was completely destroyed by the "Gongping" vessel. The cargo that fell into the water was later retrieved. The boatmen on the cargo barge jumped onto the dock and were fortunately unharmed.

Aftermath

After the incident, the Jinhongsheng cargo barge fortunately

was close to the dock and did not sink. It was towed to a sheltered area of the dock. The boat captain reported the incident to the Water Police Station and prepared a list of losses in preparation for negotiating compensation. The owner of the "Gongping" vessel stated that the collision was due to an accident when the cable snapped. After the vessel was secured, he also reported to the Ship Department and General Manager Liu.

Two Female Doctors at Shangxian Tang Women and Children's Hospital Accused of Negligence, Wife of "Shibao" Employee Dies Tragically in Hospital, Indicted for Manslaughter

Ge Chenghui and Zhu Changya, two female doctors at the Shangxian Tang Women and Children's Hospital on Avenue Sa Po Se in the French Concession, have recently been privately sued in the Second Special District Court by Shen Wenda, an employee of the "Shibao" newspaper, on charges of manslaughter, requesting an investigation. The details were briefly reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, a summons was issued, and Judge Xiong Huiping presided over the hearing in the Second Criminal Court. Jin Xiongbo, the representative of the plaintiff, stated that the plaintiff suffered a major shock after the tragic death of his wife and was spitting blood, so he did not appear in court. The plaintiff's wife, Li, was sent to the Shangxian Tang Women and Children's Hospital last month for childbirth. At that time, the pregnant woman was in good health. Doctors Ge Chenghui and Zhu Changya were responsible for the delivery. By the next day, the baby had not been born and the amniotic fluid had broken. When the plaintiff inquired of others, he was told that once the amniotic fluid broke, it was important to seek medical treatment quickly, and any delay could be fatal. The plaintiff was greatly alarmed and rushed to ask the first defendant, Ge Chenghui, if she had any confidence in delivering the baby, when it would be born, and if there were any risks. Otherwise, he would transfer to another hospital. Ge replied solemnly that the hospital had considerable experience and guaranteed there would be no danger. The plaintiff was greatly relieved. However, on the 29th, he was suddenly told that the pregnant woman's condition was not good. The plaintiff was shocked and immediately called Dr. Zhong Shuzhen for a consultation, who said that there was no way to save her. The defendants then took advantage of the plaintiff's panic and forced him to sign a document stating that life and death were determined by fate. On May 1st, both mother and child died tragically in the hospital. In these circumstances, the defendants neglected their duties and violated Article 291, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Code, requesting an investigation. Regarding the private prosecution, the plaintiff voluntarily abandoned it. The plaintiff's purpose was only to punish one as a warning to others. Defendant Ge Chenghui stated that Shen's wife was sent to the hospital on the morning of the 23rd, but she was managing the outpatient clinic downstairs and Dr. Zhu Changya was responsible for the plaintiff's wife. Occasionally, the plaintiff asked her to check on his wife's condition. At that time, the pregnant woman could eat and speak, and her condition was very good. However, on the 29th, she suddenly changed, but she was at the countryside visiting the doctor, so she did not know the circumstances of Li's death. However, there is a daily treatment chart for Li in the hospital, which can be presented as evidence for inspection. Zhu Changya said that Shen's wife came to the hospital and she was responsible for her. Her condition was usually very good, but she suddenly changed on the 29th. With the plaintiff's consent, Dr. Zhong was asked to invite Dr. Cai to the scene for treatment, but there was no way to save her. Judge Tai ordered them to leave and rescheduled a hearing to summon Dr. Zhong and Dr. Cai to testify.

Jiangnan Shipyard's No. 3 Dock Will Soon Be Completed

According to the North China Daily News, the Jiangnan Shipyard, which is under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of the Navy, was established 69 years ago. In the third year after the opening of the factory, the No. 1 dock was built, which was 325 feet long. After many years, it was expanded to 375 feet. Later, because ships of more than 4,000 tons could not enter the dock for repairs, it was expanded to its current capacity, which is 545 feet long, 66 feet wide, and 20 feet deep. In the winter of 1925, the No. 2 dock was completed, equipped with new-style machinery. The dock is 502 feet long, 61 feet wide, and 23 feet deep, but it still cannot accommodate ships of more than 10,000 tons. Currently, with the development of Shanghai's port and the increasing number of ship repair projects, the factory authorities requested the Ministry of the Army to allocate a large area of land from the site of the Jiangnan Manufacturing Bureau for expansion. It was finally decided to build a 600-foot-long dry dock. Later, due to the outbreak of the January 28th Incident and financial constraints, the authorities had to change the original plan and decided to carry out the project in two stages. First, a smaller dock was built to meet the needs. Once it was completed, the second phase of the project would be carried out, and the total length would reach 600 feet, the width 100 feet, and the depth 26 feet, which would be able to accommodate ships of more than 10,000 tons and would be the largest of Shanghai's docks. The newly built dock, the No. 3 dock of the factory, is 375 feet long, 89 feet wide, and 26 feet deep. It was originally scheduled to be completed at the beginning of this month, but it has been postponed twice due to bad weather and will be completed in September. The first phase of the project is estimated to cost 1.2 million yuan.

Prize Drawing for Resolute Brand Thermoses

Bright Company - 10th Anniversary

Bright Manufacturing of Thermoses and Electrical Appliances Co., Ltd., located at 128 Museum Road in this city, is celebrating its 10th anniversary this year. To mark the occasion, it issued prize tickets, which have been selling exceptionally well. The company, in compliance with regulations, held the drawing yesterday at the Shanghai Bankers' Association. Attendees included Lin Kanghou, Wen Lanting, Pan Gongzhan, Wang Zikang, Pan Xulun, Chao Jimei, Zhang Qinxian, Pan Yangyao, Chen Riping, Feng Shaoshan, representatives Feng Langao and Wang Jiean, representative Chen Zian, Dr. Xia Shaoping, Lu Yuan, and over a hundred other guests. The gathering was lively and impressive. The meeting commenced at 2 PM, chaired by Liang Bozhi, Manager of the company, with Dr. Xia Shaoping as the master of ceremonies and Zhang Qinxian as the recorder. Chairman Liang reported, "Ladies and gentlemen, today is the day our company celebrates its 10th anniversary. We are honored by your presence and guidance, and my colleagues and I are deeply grateful. I feel somewhat ashamed that we don't have much to commemorate at this anniversary, but I will briefly report on the past ten years in two points. First, regarding thermoses in China ten years ago, when our company was first established, all thermoses on the market were imported. In terms of usage, inferior goods were obviously not suitable. While Western products were usable, they were very expensive, costing six, seven, or eight yuan each, making them inaccessible to the general public. Seeing this situation, we established our company ten years ago to manufacture thermoses, aiming to resist foreign goods and reduce imports. This goal was strongly supported by Minister Kong Xiangxi when he visited our factory five years ago. At the same time, we sought to make this hygienic product available to the entire nation. Our company considers this worthy of commemoration. Second, regarding the technology for manufacturing thermoses in China ten years ago, there were no factories or specialized personnel for making thermoses. Our company felt this was shameful, so we decided to use Chinese capital and domestic technicians to manufacture thermoses ourselves, sparing no expense in painstaking research. Although we had some success twelve or thirteen years ago, the manufacturing quality could not match Western products, so we chose to sacrifice profits and not sell them on the market, upholding our belief in elevating the status of domestic goods. By 1923, our company finally achieved excellent results. As soon as our products were launched, they became popular throughout the country and in Southeast Asia, receiving a warm welcome from all sectors of society. We also used various technologies to reduce prices and contribute to society, aiming for widespread use, making it a household necessity. Our company also considers this technology, which has had a great effect on public health, to be worthy of commemoration. These are the two points I wanted to report. This year marks our 10th anniversary, hence this celebration. However, ten years is a very short time. Just like a child from birth to ten years old is still in a very immature stage and cannot be considered an adult, our company feels the same way. We dare not be complacent and continue to work hard, and we sincerely hope for your continued support." Following this, Pan Gongzhan and Lin Kanghou delivered speeches, expressing their appreciation for the company's efforts over the past decade. At 3 PM, Lin Kanghou, Wang Xiaolai, Wang Jiean, representative Chen Zian, Feng Shaoshan, representative Feng Langao, and Wen Lanting supervised the drawing, with Chen Riping, an accounting expert, conducting the process. The winning numbers announced were: First Prize: 108870; Second Prize: 170052; Third Prize: 188778, 146212, 170325, 167999, etc. Fourth and Fifth Prizes were awarded based on the last four or two digits matching the First and Second Prize numbers. It is reported that the First Prize winner receives a round-trip first-class ticket to America.

Meiya Silk Weaving Factory Exhibits Fashion at the National Products Department Store, Holding a Lantern Festival for Three Consecutive Days Starting Yesterday

The Meiya Silk Weaving Factory in this city, recognizing the influx of foreign goods in recent years, believes that only by vigorously promoting national products can the situation be salvaged. Therefore, it has innovatively manufactured high-quality silk fabrics and is promoting them in the market. This year, China's silk industry has suffered due to the dumping of Japanese silk in Europe and America, leading to a slump. Silk prices have fallen daily, and the cost of silk products has gradually decreased, making silk fabrics inexpensive and comparable to foreign cloth prices. Recently, the factory has launched various new and innovative summer silk fabrics. To expand promotion, it is jointly holding a fashion display and lantern festival with the China National Products Company at the Continental Department Store, starting yesterday for a total of three days. The events will take place three times a day at 10 AM, 2 PM, and 6 PM, with a 10% discount for three days. The factory has hired six beautiful women to wear the newly produced fashions, sitting or standing on carts, which are pushed by apprentices from the Puyi Training Institute. Minutes of the Rickshaw Guild General Meeting

The Special District Office of the Rickshaw Guild of this city convened an emergency general meeting of all members yesterday afternoon at 2 PM. Over eighty people attended, including Gu Songmao, Hou Shaoan, Yin Zhiling, La Hegao, and Zhu Suiyuan. At 4 PM, the meeting was called to order, and Yin Zhiling was elected chairman. After the formalities, the chairman first reported on the situation of contacting the Public Works Department regarding the standard new rickshaw design. Next, the following motions were discussed: (1) The Public Rickshaw Management Office of the Public Works Department announced that from today onwards, any new rickshaws must conform to the standard new design. If the office does not approve, the rickshaw license will not be issued, causing the old-style rickshaw shells and parts that the rickshaw owners have prepared to be completely discarded and useless, amounting to bankruptcy. Regarding the method of responding to this situation, Gu Songmao reported that adding a black canopy with cloth lining, armrests on both sides of the seat, and using paint and cotton padding to the original rickshaw shell, if approved, would prevent the old-style rickshaw shells that the owners had prepared from being completely useless. It was resolved to have the board of directors draft a new rickshaw design and submit it to the Management Office for adoption, so that while respecting the solemnity of the Public Rickshaw Management Office's announcement, the interests of the rickshaw owners would not be harmed. (2) A motion to organize a cooperative to ensure uniformity in the painting of new rickshaws was passed. The board of directors was tasked with determining the specific methods. (3) Gu Songmao proposed that the Public Works Department had sixteen articles regarding rickshaw issues. Except for the first, second, and third articles, which were reserved, there were thirteen other articles. If these were all announced one by one in announcements, the rickshaw owners would be overwhelmed. A motion to send representatives to participate in the management office's coordination to facilitate progress was passed. The board of directors was instructed to send representatives to participate. (4) Regarding the special donations raised for relief, which were originally kept by Xu Liangbi, Hu Rongwang, Wang Kunyi, and Liu Shengwu, as Director Liu Shengwu has not attended meetings for a long time, a motion to nominate a replacement was passed. Zhu Suiyuan was nominated to jointly manage the funds. (5) Regarding the re-verification of registration certificates by this office, the board of directors decided to issue new certificates and nominated standing director Yin Zhiling, registration committee member Hou Shaoan, and review committee member Bao Guoxiang to be responsible for signing and stamping the certificates. A motion that the issuance of certificates should be subject to the retroactive approval of this general meeting was passed. Gu Songmao and Liang Ruiting were added as registration committee members. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 PM.

"Manchukuo" Judged Under the Doctrine of the Catholic Church

Newly Published by the Sacred Teaching Magazine

Mr. Lu Zhengxiang, former Prime Minister and Minister of Foreign Affairs, now a Benedictine monk in Belgium, recently wrote an article in French entitled "Manchukuo Judged Under the Doctrine of the Catholic Church." The Sacred Teaching Magazine of Xujiahui has translated it into Chinese and published it as a separate booklet. It can be obtained from the magazine for a postage fee of three cents. Mr. Lu wrote this book to correct the European and American misunderstanding of China caused by the negative propaganda of Japan. He distributed the book to political circles in various countries, thereby correcting many misunderstandings. Furthermore, the Catholic doctrine described in the book is based on Cardinal Mercier of Belgium's remarks on the German army's occupation of Belgium during the European War, which deeply reflects the current situation of our country and is sufficient to warn the powers that are invading us.

Li Jushi's Edited "Theory and Practice of Controlled Economy" - Fourteenth Volume of the New China Construction Society Series

Since its establishment, the New China Construction Society of Shanghai has been actively engaged in promoting academic research and national revival, making significant contributions to the country and society. However, it usually does not engage in ostentation, but seeks to establish a solid foundation, so the outside world is not very aware of its activities. However, the society's publications, such as the regularly published "Fuxing Monthly," have seen a sharp increase in sales due to their substantial content. In addition, the society has published a series of books, including (1) "A Collection of Japanese Views on Our Northeast," (2) "Military Aviation," (3) "The Soviet Union's Five-Year Plan," (4) "Xingguo Records (First Collection)," (5) "Historical Materials on the Constitution of the Republic of China," (6) "A History of International Intelligence," (7) "The World Economic Situation Since the European War," (8) "A Study of Electoral Systems in Various Countries," (9) "An Economic Survey of Chahar," (10) "Scientific Modern War Preparation," (11) "Educational Systems and Overview of Various Countries," (12) "Recent Northeast Economy and Japan," and (13) "Currency Policies and Currency Wars of Various Countries," for a total of thirteen kinds. Most of these have been welcomed and loved by the general public, with many reprints and third editions. Recently, a book entitled "Theory and Practice of Controlled Economy," edited by Li Jushi, was also published at the inauguration ceremony of the society's new headquarters (on the 27th). The content is extremely rich, including an introduction, the meaning of controlled economy, the development of controlled economy theory, the reasons for the rise of controlled economy, the goals of controlled economy, the content of controlled economy, and fifteen chapters on Germany, Italy, the Soviet Union, England, the United States, France, Japan, Japan, "Manchukuo," and China. The entire book is over 300,000 words, printed in a 23-size format. The book selects new materials and uses concise language to provide a systematic and organized description of controlled economy. The introduction of theory is extremely accurate, and the explanation of the actual application in various countries is particularly comprehensive and concise. Since the concept of controlled economy has swept the globe, many Chinese people have sought to solve national problems through this path. However, although there is a vast amount of publications on this topic, there are not many that are relatively complete and substantial. Li Jushi's compilation fills this gap. The book is prefaced by Mr. Huang Fu, the current Chairman of the Beiping Political Consolidation Committee, Mr. Jin Guobao, a member of the Guangxi Economic Committee and Deputy Manager of the Shanghai Jiaotong Bank, Dr. Zhang Sumin, a professor at National Jinan University, Mr. Tang Qingzeng, Dean of the Business School of Daxia University and Editor-in-Chief of the Quarterly Journal of Economics of the Chinese Economic Society, and Mr. Dong Xiujia, Dean of the Business School of National Jinan University and former Director of the Jiangsu Construction Department, all of whom are contemporary scholars with a wealth of knowledge. They have all highly praised the book, and it has been carefully reviewed by economic expert Dr. Li Quanshi, demonstrating its value. Therefore, anyone who aspires to study controlled economy must read this book. It is also suitable as an economic reference book for universities and high schools. The price is 1.60 yuan per copy. It is sold at major bookstores nationwide, or you can contact the publishing department of the society at 656 Weihaiwei Road, Shanghai (telephone 95663). There are preferential terms for schools, institutions, and libraries nationwide.

Bank Inspection Report Compilation

The Central Bank's 198th Report on the Inspection of Issuance Reserves states: This council, according to Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, is responsible for inspecting the reserves for exchange notes issued by this bank. The 198th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of this bank on May 31st of the 23rd year of the Republic of China. The results of the inspection are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of silver dollar exchange notes issued: 71,100,120 yuan, including: 64,463,739 yuan in silver dollar notes, 6,465,281 yuan in subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of exchange note reserves: 71,100,120 yuan, including: 57,915,020 yuan in cash reserves. The cash reserves include 54,400,264 yuan stored in this bank's issuing vault, 1,710,646 yuan stored in various branches, and 1,802,210 yuan stored with fellow banks. Guarantee reserves converted to 13,186,000 yuan in silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold unit exchange notes issued: 373,324.70 yuan. Total amount of customs gold unit exchange note reserves: 373,324.70 yuan. These reserves include 7,351.95 taels of standard gold, which, at a fixed price of 0.50779, equals 373,324.70 yuan in customs gold units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Exchange Note Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the guarantee reserve 40%. The results of this inspection show that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This is hereby reported. June 1st, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Chairman of the Board of Supervisors of the Central Bank, Li Fusun, Supervisors Xie Mingxun, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Qia Qing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jiji.

The China General Chamber of Commerce Bank's Issuance Reserve Inspection Report states: The China General Chamber of Commerce Bank's exchange note issuance and reserve funds for May of the 23rd year have been inspected by supervisors Fu Qilin, He Shaoyin, Xie Jishan, and Zhang Boqin, together with accountant Xu Yongzuo, on June 1st. The results of the inspection are listed below: Total amount of exchange notes issued: 18,482,100 yuan. Total amount of reserves: 18,482,100 yuan, including: 13,392,600 yuan in cash reserves, exceeding 60%, and 5,089,500 yuan in guarantee reserves, less than 40%. Both comply with the issuance regulations.

The First Inspection Report on the Issuance Reserves in the Shanghai Area of the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank states: The issuance of exchange notes by the China Agricultural and Industrial Bank has always been completely separate from the business department. It is now reported that the bank has organized a Shanghai Area Issuance Reserve Inspection Committee to make the issuance reserves public. The first inspection was held on May 31st. Accountant Tang Zaizhang, together with representatives from the leading note-issuing banks, jointly inspected the numbers of all issued exchange notes, cash reserves, and guarantee reserves, which are listed on the left: Exchange notes, including the total amount issued by this bank and used by leading banks, totaled 5,469,982 yuan. Cash reserves: 3,989,264 yuan (equivalent to 73%). Guarantee reserves: 1,480,718 yuan (equivalent to 27%). The above two items were inspected and found to be accurate and in compliance with the regulations. This is hereby announced.

Dear Editor, I have checked the June 1st issue of your newspaper and found that it stated that Shen Zongquan, the Tenth District Party Headquarters executive committee member, and school groups, etc., organized a New Life Movement conference and held a grand parade the night before, which is inconsistent with the facts. After investigating, the district party headquarters promoted the New Life Movement and held an expanded publicity campaign on May 15th. The lantern parade was completely voluntary by various businesses. Moreover, Shen Zongquan was originally the captain of the security team and was not an executive committee member of the district party headquarters. I am corresponding to request that the newspaper make corrections. Sincerely, the editorial department of this port news of the Shen Bao, Wang Yonggong, Standing Committee Member of the Tenth District Party Headquarters, June 1st

Reading Q&A

On "Humor"

│││By Li Qiushi│││

What is the explanation of "humor"? Does humorous literature have a place in the literary field?

Lately, we have often seen letters from readers, like Mr. Li Qiushi, raising questions like these to us. Because they have discovered that many publications currently contain argumentative articles on humorous literature, it has aroused their interest in this question. At the same time, they feel the need for a thorough understanding. In order to meet the requirements of our readers, we cannot help but raise this question and give a simple and clear explanation.

What is called "humor"? "Humor" is originally a transliteration of the English word "Humor." Generally speaking, it contains two elements: satire and mockery. It is a form of mockery, but at the same time, it feels sorrow for the one being mocked; or, although it is laughable, it can evoke understanding and compassion. Therefore, mockery that does not contain satire or educational meaning cannot be counted as humor. When we see Charlie Chaplin's strange appearance, it is of course laughable, but what we cannot forget most is the strong satire that is set off from his appearance. When we see the clowns in old Chinese operas, they are sometimes funny, but what we should not ignore most is the invisible warning that it gives us. Without the essence of humor, everything about Charlie Chaplin and the clowns would only degenerate into slapstick and nonsense.

Some people regard humor as the key to self-preservation and self-cultivation, as a form of entertainment for themselves, so they believe that: not talking about the universe, but only talking about "flies" is humor. This is a misunderstanding, and it can even be said to be a defamation of humor. Of course, from "flies," it is not impossible to recognize the reality of society, but what we must remember is that talking about flies and talking about the universe are still exploring the truth and still reflecting one aspect of reality. Obviously, the question is not about talking about "flies" or talking about the universe, but about how to attach the meaning of education or satire to the mockery. What we are talking about is whether we have fulfilled the task of education or satire. Otherwise, learning to pretend to be Charlie Chaplin's "honorable appearance" is actually just a low-level fun. Some people also believe that "humor" is just a trick played by cowardly gentlemen. The general public does not need humor. If they want to laugh, they can laugh wildly. If they want to scold, they can scold loudly. They don't need any politeness. This is also an overly mechanical view. They treat the public as abstract and as a uniform thing, and ignore the various components of the public, which require various different types of education; they need to be enlightened from the expression of the correct world view and outlook on life. How can you say that the public does not need humor? For anyone, a direct satire and admonishment are most likely to cause disgust. Once there is disgust, its effectiveness will inevitably be reduced. If we express the content of satire in gentle laughter, then the listener will feel comfortable, and the influence they receive invisibly will definitely be deeper than direct satire. Humor is the best way to educate the public. It is a mirror that can point out various shortcomings and teach how to correct those shortcomings. Humor is not retreat, but still an attack, a side attack. The opinions of the two families above only see the appearance of humor and overlook the essence of humor.

Then, does it have a place in the field of literature? We can resolutely answer: yes, humor is the main component of comedy. In our era, tragedies that describe the pain of the era are of course necessary, but humorous comedies that educate the public have a more important meaning. We certainly do not deny that the humor that is currently being promoted does not contain this meaning at all, but we cannot deny the existence of humor because of this. Our main task is to restore humor from the perverted state of slapstick and nonsense to its original appearance and take on its actual task. We can repeat once more, humorous literature that educates the public is bound to exist!

The Fifth China Middle School Sports Federation Games Opened Yesterday Two High Jumps from Shangzhong were Outstanding Surprising Upsets Final Broke Records Total of Five Items

The track and field competition of the Fifth Middle School Games, organized by the Shanghai Secondary School Sports Federation, began at the China Track and Field Field at 2:00 PM yesterday. (Track and Field Snippets)

The men's 100 meters and 200 meters held semi-finals yesterday. Zeng Rongzhong of Jinan and Dong Yinchu of Guanghua both won their groups. Their results were similar. Today, the competition between these two tigers will be fierce. Zeng is known for his speed, while Huang is known for his explosive power. It's hard to say who will win. The men's 400 meters held no preliminary round yesterday due to the small number of participants. Zeng Rongzhong led from start to finish, ultimately winning first place with 53.6 seconds, breaking the highest record of 54.8 seconds held by Long Xueqiu.

30 people participated in the men's 1500 meters. Long-distance runner Wang Zhengling also participated in the competition. In the first lap, Lan Shijie of Fuzhong led, followed by Gu Xinbing of Daxia. Wang was in third place. After the second lap, Wang broke out into first place. Lan dropped out midway. Gu Binghou and Zhou Songxian were in second place. The order remained the same in the third lap. In the fourth lap, as they approached the finish line, Zhao Miaogen of Yuqing emerged from behind, finishing in second place, only ten meters behind Wang Zhengling.

The men's 400-meter relay was participated in by six schools: Shangzhong, Yuqing, Hujiang, Nanshang, Daxia, and Guanghua. Yuqing had the advantage in the first leg. After the second leg, Feng Yuqi of Hujiang sprinted desperately, ultimately winning first place by maintaining his effort until the finish line. Yuqing was second, Shangzhong was third, and Daxia was fourth, with a result of 48.54 seconds.

In the men's high jump and long jump, Shangzhong pulled off a surprise. Zhou Shilong broke the record of 1.69 meters held by Li Lin and Xie Jinhe in the high jump with 1.725 meters. Feng Wenchang broke the record of 6.206 meters held by Wang Jihua in the long jump with 6.605 meters. This was truly unexpected.

At that time, they may be able to compete for a place. Competition Method: Each team will be scored based on the top six finishers. The one with the fewest points wins (using the reverse calculation method). Each team is limited to a maximum of ten participants. Those who withdraw midway will be counted as the last place. Primary schools have not yet been adequately developed; how can they withstand this? Education News

Yunnan Education Director Gong Zizhi Discusses Promoting Education in Border Areas

Yunnan Education Director Gong Zizhi arrived at the Ministry of Education on the 31st to meet with Vice Minister Duan and Director Gu to explain a plan to promote education in border areas. Afterwards, it was reported that the director intends to gradually complete education in border areas within six years in three stages. The initial plan is to establish five simple normal schools in various border areas of Yunnan to train teachers for promotion purposes. One will be established in Deqin (in the northwest corner of Yunnan, inhabited by Tibetans), focusing on Tibetan language instruction due to its environment. Second, one will be established in Mianning (in the southwest, inhabited by the Yi people), focusing on Lolo language instruction. Third, one will be established in Cheli (due south, inhabited by the Yi people and near Myanmar, Siam, and Annam), focusing on Burmese language instruction. Fourth, one will be established in Zhaotong (in the northeast corner, inhabited by ethnic minorities), focusing on Lolo language instruction. Fifth, one will be established in Qiubei (in the southeast, inhabited by the Miao and Yao people), focusing on Miao language instruction. In addition, in terms of public education, schools and social-style public education centers will be established, and itinerant lectures and educational films will be used as promotional tools. The initial plan is to establish one to two hundred public schools, with a total cost of approximately 40,000 yuan. Requests for subsidies have been made to Executive Yuan President Wang and educational circles, and it is decided to begin implementation in August after the summer break this year. Regardless of the extent of financial subsidies and provincial fundraising, at a minimum, the simple normal schools in Deqin, Mianning, and Cheli must be established, and public schools will also be established as much as possible, separately.

Honors for Chinese Writers: Chen Sanli and Hu Shi Elected Honorary Members of PEN

The PEN Club was founded by the British female writer Mrs. Dawson Scott. Poets, playwrights, essayists, novelists, and editors are all eligible for membership. The headquarters are located in London. The first president was Mr. Galsworthy, and the honorary member was Hardy. Both have now passed away. The current president is the famous H.G. Wells. PEN Clubs have been established in twenty-eight countries around the world. In total only forty famous writers from various countries have been elected as honorary members of the London PEN Club. From China, Chen Sanli and Hu Shi were recently elected as honorary members by the association. Shen Bao Radio Weekly

Radio Silence Control Method

— Yi Zhi

Recently, new American radios, in addition to using sensitive automatic volume controls, also have silence controls. Their function is to prevent a kind of noise from entering the antenna and being input into the speaker to cause annoyance before the radio receives an external signal.

The principle of the silence controller is to use the Class B amplification characteristics of a vacuum tube, that is, to make the grid receive a considerable negative voltage, so that the plate current is cut off, which is equal to zero. The low-frequency amplifier tube then loses its working effect, so even a slight noisy sound on the grid cannot be input into the speaker and make a sound. Now, let's give an example to explain it, please look at the diagram. VI is the automatic volume control tube, V2 is the silence adjustment tube (Silent tuning tube), V3 is the low-frequency strong amplification tube, R, R1, R2 are fixed load resistors. R3 is the volume control, R4 is the silence control. When the radio is turned on but has not received an external signal, the automatic volume control does not work, and the R load resistor has no voltage drop. Therefore, the control grid of the silence adjustment tube does not receive a negative voltage (R1 is an isolation load resistor and has no voltage drop), the plate current is very large, and the voltage drop of the R2 load resistor is also very large. Because of this, the grid of the low-frequency strong amplification tube receives a considerable negative voltage, the plate current is cut off here, and the speaker does not make a sound. But if an external signal comes, the automatic volume control immediately takes over the work, there is a negative voltage on the R load resistor, the grid of the silence adjustment tube receives this considerable negative voltage, and the plate current immediately decreases, and the voltage drop of the R2 load resistor also decreases. Since the negative voltage received by the grid of the low-frequency amplifier tube is small, the plate current will not be cut off, and it will perform its amplification work. On the one hand, after the external signal is rectified by the automatic volume control tube, a low-frequency voltage is generated on the R load resistor. After passing through the capacitor C1 to R3, the appropriate volume is adjusted and input into the low-frequency amplifier tube, amplified to the speaker, and the original signal is generated. As for the adjustment of the R4 silence controller, because the received signal has strong and weak, and the noise entering the antenna is also of different sizes, it must be tested and adjusted to the appropriate place.

How to Improve a Radio: Adding an Adjustment Indicator

— Yong Yan

On the panel of new radios, there is often a visible adjustment indicator (Visual tuning meter). This thing is to help with the adjustment, so that you can get the maximum volume and the clearest sound quality. The principle is also very simple, it uses an instrument that can indicate the strength of the current, the instrument is placed in a circuit that is related to the strength of the radio signal received. Usually a sensitive ammeter is used, connected to the plate circuit of one or more high-frequency amplification vacuum tubes. When this vacuum tube has not received a radio signal, the reading indicated by this ammeter is the plate current of this vacuum tube at the plate voltage used. However, when a radio signal is received, its plate current also changes accordingly: the greater the change in this plate current, the more legal the adjustment is. At this time, the pointer of the ammeter connected to the plate circuit will naturally move with the change in current. When we are adjusting, we only need to make the pointer of this indicating ammeter rotate to the maximum to get the maximum volume and the best tone.

If the adjustment of a heterodyne or automatic volume control radio is not correct, the sound quality is very poor, so an adjustment indicator is really necessary. If there is enough space on the panel of the radio to add an adjustment indicator, you can add it according to the attached diagram. You only need to break the plate circuit of the high-frequency amplification stage vacuum tube and add a direct current milliampere as shown in the figure. However, the current passing through this ammeter must not be greater than the maximum current that this ammeter can measure; at the same time, the positive and negative connections must not be confused, otherwise the pointer will point backwards.

Talking Again About New Pocket Radios

— Jian Cun

The previous issue of this journal (Issue 64) contained the new pocket radio published by Mr. Silian. Because the values of the required components were not specified in the diagram, and the principle of operation of the machine was not mentioned, readers have been writing to inquire recently. In addition to answering them separately, I will repeat the values of the required parts and the principle of operation in order to supplement the shortcomings of the previous article.

R7=1meg·n R8=1500n R9=2300n R10=330n C14=0、000 R1=1、5mcg、n R2=1mcg·n R3=0mcg·n R4=1、5mcg·n R5=1·5mcg·n R6=0·3mcg·n C5=0·02 C6=40uf C7=0·00、5uf C8=0、006uf C9=0、007uf C10=0、005uf C11 C12=8、5uf L1=3、4mh（40n）·L2=0、27mh（10n） L3 L4=0、28mh（3、5n） L5=5、3mh（un） C=C10 C2=0、00032mh C=0、00026 C=0、037mh

Circuit mode; The circuit used in this machine is shown in the first diagram, and the values of the parts used are also listed in the diagram. However, the one shown in the first diagram is slightly different from the one published by Mr. Silian, because the circuit used by Mr. Silian is applicable to explaining the principle, and this diagram is its actual circuit. There is nothing special about the circuit mode used, but two vacuum tubes are used as the function of a four-tube type, and the order of operation is radio frequency first stage, amplification, detection, and audio frequency second stage amplification. Now I will describe it in more detail below.

The antenna circuit uses C14 (fixed capacitor for antenna) and L1 (primary coil for antenna) for series tuning, but the capacitance of C14 is slightly larger, and a coil of about one turn is made from one end of L1 to intersect with the tuning circuit for radio frequency amplification.

Radio frequency amplification detection, audio frequency amplification and other functions are handled by one 6F7 tube. The radio frequency amplification tuning circuit is formed by C1 and L3, which is a complete and independent circuit, and is closely coupled with the L2 coil in the control grid circuit of the pentode part of the 6F7 tube, that is, L2 and L3 are wound on the same cylinder. The radio frequency amplified by the pentode part of the 6F7 tube passes through C6 and intersects with the grid of the triode part of the same tube. The tuning circuit is C2L4 and then C3R5 is used for grid detection. The audio frequency current after detection flows to the plate circuit of the triode part, and causes an audio frequency voltage at both ends of R3. The voltage passes through C4 and returns to the control grid of the pentode part to complete the audio frequency amplification and complete its reflex circuit. After that, the audio frequency voltage is supplied to the control grid of the pentode part of the 12A7 tube through ordinary load resistance coupling, and after being amplified by it, it is input to the speaker for operation.

The diode part in the 12A7 tube is used as a rectifier tube to perform the rectification function. The resistance R9 is used to replace the filter choke coil, and the capacitors C12 and C13 for filtering each use a value of 3uf.

The reason why this radio is different from other radios is that the 6F7 input circuit uses an inductive coupling method. This coil is made of a special wire. The center of the wire is a hard wire, and its surroundings have nine strands of mutually insulated stranded wire. The hard single wire in the center is used as the grid wire and connected to the tuning capacitor. The nine stranded wires on the outside are connected to the input grid of the vacuum tube. Also, because the machine strives for small size, the variable capacitor used is also manufactured differently from ordinary ones. The rest of the parts also try to avoid being bulky. The values of the parts are marked in the figure, so I won’t go into details here.

Radio Using Two 33 Tubes

— Zhu Ziyuan

Because there is no electricity in the interior, AC machines have never been popular. Except for a few research comrades who are experimenting with installation, it is simply one in a hundred. Therefore, DC machines can fill the interior, especially the power-saving type is the most popular. Therefore, 30, 31, 32, 33, and other vacuum tubes are the best-selling in my hometown, Songjiang.

The combination of one 30 detection and two 30 low-frequency amplifications has gradually been eliminated. Recently, the combination of one 30 detection and one 33 strong low-frequency amplification has become very popular. The reason is that the start-up cost is simple, the location is economical, and the volume is better than two 30 low-frequency amplifications, so everyone is happy to install it. However, since the 33 detection single-tube horn circuit was published in the newspaper, everyone has abandoned the old and welcomed the new for installation. The author is also one of the testers, but the test results show that in Songjiang, it is good to receive Shanghai's 100-watt stations, but the volume of small power stations is insufficient, and the effect is not as good as one 30 detection and 33 strong low-frequency amplification. So I added a stage of strong low-frequency amplification using 33, and successfully created a radio with two 33 tubes. The result was amazing. Its loudness is far beyond what 30 detection and 33 low-frequency amplification can achieve. I once took it to the noisy city and put the speaker at the door of a relative's store. It could be heard from more than a dozen storefronts away. Its loudness is comparable to that of a five-tube AC machine. Now more people are installing it. The author has installed two pairs for relatives, and Comrade Cai has also installed several for others. The effects are all very good and have never failed, so I dare to introduce it in this journal. Please come and try it out, fellow enthusiasts.

As shown in the figure, it is a stage of regenerative detection, plus a stage of low-frequency amplification, and there is nothing special about it. The capacitance of the parts are marked in the figure, and readers can refer to it. What should be noted is the C voltage problem, because after the high-power output here, there is another stage of high-power transformer-coupled low-frequency amplification, so it is very easy to cause distortion. The C voltage must be adjusted very carefully in order to get good results. Here, 135V is just an approximate number. Readers need to add more or subtract more to try to get the strongest volume without distortion.

Because this machine uses transformer-coupled low-frequency amplification, the sound is very loud, but the chance of distortion is also relatively high, so here we attach great importance to the C voltage. Please do not ignore it, readers. I think if you use resistance-coupled low-frequency amplification, although the volume will be reduced, the chance of distortion may be eliminated. If you have time, you may also try it!

Wireless Radio Tidbits

— Zhifan

Regarding the phenomenon of shortwave skip distance, according to a veteran in the wireless radio field, this phenomenon does not exist within our country. A shortwave transmitter of 15 watts or more can communicate unimpeded throughout the nation. The reason for this is probably due to our country's climate having extremely high humidity.

Overseas communication is often superior to landline communication. However, submarines can only communicate with long waves when they are 60 feet below the surface, and cannot communicate at all below 100 feet. The reason for this has yet to be satisfactorily explained.

The dry battery type 32 vacuum tube is a screen grid type power amplifier and detector tube. Its operational performance is highly inconsistent. Therefore, special attention must be paid to the voltage of its screen grid during application. Experiment with various voltages (from 22.5 to 67 volts) to find the most suitable value. Relying on what is said in books or magazines will unlikely yield good results. When used as a detector in a typical regenerative circuit, this vacuum tube is not as effective as the type 34. Gentlemen, you may wish to try it out.

The 245 vacuum tube is a newly released power amplification tube. Based on my personal testing, I find that its effectiveness is not significantly better than the type 47, and it is quite prone to damage. The B voltage is typically 250 volts, but I have changed it to 220 volts. The volume is not reduced, and it should be more durable.

Imported radios are subject to price reductions due to competition in the market and to cater to the psychology of the Chinese people. As a result, the quality is inevitably lowered. China's climate is relatively humid, especially during the yellow plum season. The insulation of transformers, filter capacitors, carbon resistors, etc., inside the machine also decreases, leading to damage. This often results in the machine's components, such as vacuum tubes, being burnt out, resulting in a loss that cannot be recovered. Even if it is not damaged, there will be excessive noise, and the radio reception will deteriorate drastically. This serves as a warning to those who are greedy for cheap goods!

Last month, the import of substandard wireless radio components reached 1.5 million yuan. Those who heard this were shocked. Examining the contents, spare parts accounted for the majority. Amateur enthusiasts who hear this should be deeply vigilant!
