Spring and Autumn

Records of Lingering Fragrance

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling, translated by Qin Shouou

Only when the Empress Dowager casually had a whim and suddenly wanted to listen to music, these musicians would have to immediately start playing. This was still considered a temporary impulse. Normally, there were also several rigid, fixed performances, like a set of formulaic articles. For example, when the Empress Dowager was on the road, every time she got into or out of the car, music was indispensable; moreover when the Empress Dowager traveled within the Forbidden City in a palanquin, no matter how frequent the moves were, the band had to play whenever she boarded the palanquin. The music would only stop when she issued the order to depart and the palanquin began to move. As soon as the music stopped, these musicians had to quickly pack up their instruments, being careful not to make loud noises. They would hurriedly take a different route to get ahead of her, waiting at her destination. As soon as she arrived, they would start playing again to welcome her. Because these people were afraid of causing a delay, they often hurried very quickly, but the speed of the Empress Dowager's palanquin on the road was as slow as a turtle's pace, so they never failed to arrive in time. And this situation looked especially like an ordinary family's funeral procession!

The band consisted of twelve people, all eunuchs of course. They all wore a conical hat, but their hats had a red tassel, unlike the ones worn by the eunuchs carrying the palanquin. Their clothing was virtually identical. They all wore a waistcoat that was peach-colored, but without any embroidery. Their robes were purplish-red, appearing exceptionally bright. Traditionally, each of them had an assistant, not out of thoughtless extravagance, but because they were so busy that without an assistant, they couldn't manage everything themselves. (47)

Love Letter

— Ziyun

I have a colleague who recently received a letter. The name and address on the envelope were completely correct, but when he opened it, he was dumbfounded, because the letter was a love letter written to a woman. The gist of the letter was: "Since we parted, I have been missing you terribly, and I dream of you almost every night. Yesterday, I arranged to meet you at the ×× Theater, and I waited for two hours, but you didn't show up. Why are you so heartless? If I don't receive a reply within 24 hours of receiving this letter, I will prepare to jump into the Huangpu River." My colleague determined from the signature that a friend had mistakenly put the letter in the wrong envelope, causing this ridiculous situation. So he immediately wrote a reply, pretending to be the woman, and arranged to meet him at the Bund. Who knew that another letter would arrive the next day, this time asking to borrow money. This friend was truly extremely careless, mixing up the love letter with the letter asking to borrow money.

In the past, I had a friend who once wrote two letters: one was a love letter to his girlfriend, and the other was a letter to his parents at home. Unfortunately, in a moment of confusion, he put them in the wrong envelopes, sending the love letter to his parents and the family letter to his girlfriend. For a while, it became a source of amusement among his friends. What he didn't realize was that both of these letters were related to the issue of marriage. His father, seeing that he already had a girlfriend, stopped trying to find a spouse for him in his hometown, and his girlfriend, seeing that he was opposed to his parents making decisions for him, readily agreed to get engaged to him. So my friend actually benefited from his mistake. But his carelessness was similar to that of my colleague's friend.

Brief Notes on Huizhou Inksticks

— Dakua

My hometown has beautiful mountains and rivers, and famous figures have emerged in every era; moreover, it is also known for the Four Treasures of the Study (Chengxin Tang paper, Wang Boxuan brushes, Li Tinggui ink, and Old Pit stone inkstones). I love to collect old stories, and I will briefly record some notes on Huizhou inksticks:

Li Tinggui. From Yishui in the late Tang Dynasty, his original surname was Xi. To escape persecution, he followed his father (Li Chao) across the river to Shezhou. Because She County had many pine trees, the Li family became famous for their ink. The ink with the inscription "Gui" was the best, followed by "Gui," then "Gui," and the worst was "Xi Tinggui." It is also said that the ink with a double-ridged dragon pattern is excellent, while the single-ridged one is inferior. The best is the famous "Jianchun Round Cake," which does not decay even after being submerged in water for a month. The dragon pattern on the ink can also cut water.

Wu Zi, from Wuyuan in the Northern Song Dynasty, was good at making ink. The Wuyuan Chronicle records that Wu Zi's tomb is located in Huanggang Mountain in the east of the county, with a stele recording his ink-making activities.

Dai Yanheng, from Wuyuan in the Southern Song Dynasty, was recommended in the eighth year of the Shaoxing reign of Emperor Gaozong for making Fugu Dian ink and other inks. He also had ink names such as "Bi Gui" and "Wu Yu" that were passed down through the generations.

Wu Quchen, from Xiuning Shangshan in the Ming Dynasty, imitated the Yishui ink-making method and deeply understood its essence. He had an arrogant nature, and when he encountered scholars, he would generously give them ink, not being stingy at all. But if he encountered officials or wealthy merchants who wanted to exchange money for ink, he would turn a blind eye. His ink also had strange names, such as "Unmilled" and "Unprecedented." His nephew, Wu Mingwang, was also good at this, with the ink name "Zijin Shuang," known as the Two Wus. Fang Yulu, from Wuyuan in the Ming Dynasty, was good at making oxtongue ink. The best one was called "Qinglin Sui," and he wrote a book on ink recipes that was passed down through the generations.

Cheng Junfang, from Wuyuan in the Ming Dynasty, was a contemporary of Fang Yulu and also wrote a book on ink recipes. His ink making emphasized light glue, suitable for the south but not for the north. Because the north is dry, light glue cannot withstand the wind, and it is easy to break. His ink had names such as "Xuan Yuan Ling Qi."

Wang Dezi, from She County in the Ming Dynasty, made ink called "Yu Jie Chi," which was of extremely high quality, almost surpassing Cheng's ink. Unfortunately, he did not cherish it, and after his death, it was completely lost.

Low Pressure

The Art of Cursing

— Zuichisheng

There is a saying in Shanghai: "I'd rather listen to Suzhou people curse than Ningbo people talk." This shows that when it comes to the art of cursing, the Suzhou people, who are known for their "soft Wu dialect," are the most skilled. A Mr. Guanqin once wrote a joke in a newspaper about "sugar Buddha's hands." He said: The boatmen of Suzhou are the most skilled at cursing, often using terms that people don't understand. A friend of his was urinating by the river when some of his urine splashed on the stern of a boatman's boat. The boat woman saw this and cursed, "倷格隻是糖佛手㖸 (Nong ge zhi si tang fo shou a)." The friend was still baffled. Later, someone told him that she was cursing him as "堂弗收 (tang fu shou)," meaning "not to be collected in the hall," because in the past, after serious criminals were executed, their bodies had to be exposed for several days, and the charity halls would not collect them. Such is the depth of their curses. In my opinion, the next best are the people who work in brothels. I have a friend who likes to go to brothels with others, but he never wants to spend any money. Therefore, the madam often says he is "墳墩頭浪格新官人 (fen dun tou lang ge xin guan ren)," meaning "a new official on the grave mound." People hear this and don't quite understand. Later, everyone guessed that it meant he was "想發懨，死要出風頭 (xiang fa yan, si yao chu feng tou)," meaning "desperate to show off." And when they see "木林式 (mu lin shi)" customers, they call them "屋頂頭浪格菩薩 (wu ding tou lang ge pu sa)," meaning "a bodhisattva on the roof." It sounds like a respectful term, but it actually means you are "瓦老爺 (wa lao ye)," meaning "a tiled lord." This kind of "riddle-like" art of cursing is truly remarkably clever!

Four Company Commanders of the Northeast

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Nine

Returning the Letter, He Grieved and Declared His Loneliness

Listening to the Oath, They Shared Blood and Vowed Loyalty

Zi Qiang blushed and said, "How can I not go forward? I can always distinguish between public and private matters. How can I still be thinking of my family at this critical time? It's just…" He only said these two words and then stopped. Although he had stopped, Yin Deren, who was standing in front of him, knew that he couldn't go on. It would be even more difficult for him if he were to ask him about it, so he didn't say anything more. Not only was Yin Deren clear about it in his heart, but Battalion Commander Bao Fang, who was taking a walk outside to relieve the pent-up frustration in his chest, also overheard these words from across the corner. He thought to himself, if Zhao Ziqiang can't forget his love for his children, how can this battle be fought! Thinking to himself, his feet moved him along and he unconsciously walked to Tian Qing's company headquarters. There was a hole in the wall here, covered with paper to serve as a window. He looked inside and saw Tian Qing lying straight on the kang with his legs crossed, holding a photograph in his hand. It was impossible to know who was in the photograph, but after seeing him look at it, he kissed the photograph twice on the face, clearly an act of affection towards a woman. In his heart, he felt that this kind of action was even more advanced than Zhao Ziqiang's behavior. So he turned around and walked away with his hands behind his back. He walked to the end of the road and was blocked by a wall. Only then did he suddenly raise his head. As he raised his head, he heard the sound of drums in front of him. Looking, he saw two young buglers standing in the sunlight, practicing playing the drums. One hung the drum in front of his chest and beat it with drumsticks. The other tapped his feet and sang the tune of the bugle in his mouth. Just watching him swing his hands with such vigor, he had forgotten everything. Bao Fang watched for a long time. Suddenly, he turned his head and saw that the battalion commander had saluted and stood at attention. Bao Fang laughed and said, "Good boy, you're doing well. We're about to go into battle. Cheer up a bit." The bugler said, "What's the hurry? If I'm meant to die, I won't live. If I'm meant to live, I won't die." (398)

Reminiscences of Watching Lanterns

— Kedingan

In the late spring of the twenty-third year, I felt unwell, to the point of being powerless. Later, I didn't even want to eat, so I got a few days of sick leave and returned to Xinshi to recuperate. It happened that at that time, from the 30th to the 11th, many people in Xinshi were busy with the "New Life Movement Lantern Festival." Speaking of lantern festivals, the nearby places of Liuhe, Taicang, Shatou, Hengjing, Luodian, Nanxiang, Loutang, Jiaxing, and Xiashi all had their own grand occasions and their own advantages. Our Xinshi's lantern festival has always been famous. The lanterns in other places mainly use paper and are made by hand. Xinshi's lanterns are different. Their main material is Mingjing stone (also known as Thousand-Layer Paper, a mineral), which is carefully peeled open layer by layer and laid flat, then slowly ironed smooth with an iron. Then, it is carefully made into various fitting patterns with colored paper cutouts. Therefore, people with discerning eyes say that Xinshi's lanterns are more exquisite than those in other places. The most recent one was sixteen years ago, and then again thirteen years ago. At that time, I was still young and didn't have a very deep impression. There hadn't been one since. This year, the New Life Movement is popular, and the people of Xinshi didn't want to be left behind. The branches of the community raised money and each contributed ingenious works. Two months ago, they began to prepare. It is said that some of the valuable masterpieces had cost three or four thousand man-days of labor, and the least had taken dozens of man-days. Even the light and portable small works that can be held in the hand had taken twenty or thirty man-days to complete. From this, you can know the value of Xinshi's "lanterns."

I was sick and had no energy, but on the night of the first lantern festival on March 10th, I watched them to my heart's content. The opening exhibits included the New Life Movement slogan lantern from the Xinshi Public Education Center, the large incense burner from Hongfu Community (as large as the large burner in the Shanghai City God Temple), and the large Treasure Bowl, all made of Mingjing stone. The belly of the burner and the bowl were sixty inches in diameter. You can imagine how much work it took to make them with small pieces of Mingjing stone. The hexagonal pavilion from Changgeng Community, Carp Jumping Over the Dragon Gate, were also very meaningful works. Inside the pavilion was a movable mechanism of Guo Ziyi, which gave people a sense of "wealth makes people think of desires" when it moved. The carp jumping over the dragon gate jumped and jumped as if it were real. Their outer frames and all the small lanterns were all made of ironed Mingjing stone, which was very exquisite. Yongqian Community and Yong'an Community each made a large dragon boat with many figures inside, all of which could rotate. The dragon's eyes flashed, making it look majestic and terrifying. The Milky Way Bridge of Baoning Community performed the legend of the Cowherd and Weaver Girl. The Tumbling Pole Lantern was first tied to a very high bamboo frame with grids (about three rows, each with eleven grids), and each grid was hung with a different kind of lantern. The thirty-three different kinds of lanterns, all lit up and erected, were really beautiful. The silk factory of the Cooperative Community and the oil press of the Barber Community had similar mechanical movements. The Guanghan Palace of Ninghe Community was said to have taken more than three thousand man-days to complete, and its exquisite degree could set it apart. The Fengyi Pavilion and Game Pavilion of Wan'an Community each had their own merits. The Mirage of Baoan Community had its own unique insight and was extremely novel. The large lion of the Lion Dance Community was so large that it almost had to walk sideways on the narrow streets of Xinshi. Other items such as large umbrellas, small umbrellas, large and small flower baskets, etc., were produced by various communities. Especially the umbrellas, their circumference was made of colored paper cut into hexagonal or octagonal shapes, with two or three sections. The colored paper was pricked with matching landscapes, figures, insects, fish, birds, beasts, and ancient patterns with small needles. When reflected in front of the lanterns, one could see the exquisite needlework of the people of Xinshi. There were also many other fascinating lanterns that took a lot of effort to complete, but I cannot list them all.

At the head of each community, there was a silk and bamboo band or drum band to add to the fun. (The silk and bamboo music of the people of Xinshi was originally very good, and this time it was even better.)

This time, the number of spectators from the Shanghai-Hangzhou National Highway, the Jiaxing-Suzhou Waterway, and the surrounding towns and villages was no less than tens of thousands, which can be said to be an unprecedented grand occasion. Restaurants and snack shops had a booming business, but after the lantern market, the streets were still deserted. However, then again, at this time when sericulture is busy, the villagers naturally cannot come out and stroll in the streets. This is just a time of desolation! It is hoped that the farmers across the country will get some comfort this year, so that the rural economy can improve slightly!

Free Talk

How Should We Say It?

— Baige

Things always become clearer when they are discussed, and principles always become clearer when they are debated. These should be two very straightforward sentences. However, the current situation is different: Many things are clearer when they are not discussed, and become more confusing when they are discussed; they are clear when they are not debated, and become more chaotic when they are debated.

Why is this so?

This, of course, may be because the things themselves are not easily understood. Things are of all kinds, and principles can be argued in many ways. If we consider the vastness of the universe, which contains all things and principles, the universe itself is constantly changing and full of contradictions. Therefore, many things and principles have to be made more confusing and chaotic by people who each have a fixed position for certain reasons.

However, the source of this confusion and chaos lies precisely in the people who each have a fixed position. Although things are of all kinds, they always have a form, and each has its own form; although principles can be argued in many ways, they must be argued logically, and there are not many ways to argue. Even considering the universe, which is constantly changing and full of contradictions, that change and contradiction is the law upon which it depends for its existence. As long as it is not deliberately confused and distorted by people who each have a fixed position for certain interests, its true nature is very clear and easy to understand.

However, much confusion and chaos always arises from a deliberate confusion and distortion.

For example, in our intelligent literary world, there is still a mode of debate like this: If you say that someone is not good, they will say that you hate humanity and turn all of humanity against you; if you say that a certain essay is not good, they will say that you deny the existence of all essays and lightly place the crime of destroying culture on your head. Some people even extend the meaning and say that your opposition to essays is entirely due to "always feeling that small things are not pleasing to the eye."

In fact, this idea has the greatest mistake. A very clear counter-evidence is that those who attack essays, the guys who attack essays, are also essays, just a different kind. As for the so-called small things not being valued by the Chinese, that is not the whole truth: Which is more valued, "Miss" or "Elder Sister"? Are not the short Japanese rampaging in China, with even the powerful unable to do anything? Are not the tall Indians being mocked by us as Ah San? It can be seen that the words should be said differently.

So, how should we say it?

Doing One's Best

— Zhi Li

"Looking at differences, if you magnify what is large, then nothing is not large; if you diminish what is small, then nothing is not small. Knowing that heaven and earth are not grains of rice, and knowing that a fine hair can become a hill, then differences are apparent."

Although this kind of argument seems close to esoteric, it is actually the truth. Looking at the facts, the loss of the four northeastern provinces and the urgent war preparations of the great powers should be major events for the country and the world, but in the minds of most people, they have not regarded these as important. What they regard as important are flies, crickets, and the like. There are even many people who do not believe in the existence of those major events, only believing that the trivial matters related to themselves are real. This also confirms the following words: "Looking at merits, if you emphasize what is present, then nothing is not present; if you ignore what is absent, then nothing is not absent." If one's view of things is like this, how can writing be any different? There is an article in "Sanxian Ji" (Leisurely Essays) saying that in a certain environment, the author experienced a "world-weariness"-like sorrow in his heart, but it disappeared as soon as he was bitten by a mosquito. So he said: "Although it is only a mosquito bite, it is always something that happens to oneself that is more real. If I can avoid writing, I will naturally be happier. If I must write, I think I can only write about these kinds of small things, and I still cannot write them as clearly and deeply as I experienced them that day. Moreover, thousands of bites, let alone knives and guns, cannot be written."

The reason why short essays have flourished recently is also the result of the narrow scope of consciousness of the authors, which is unavoidable. However, it is different from writing the Eight-Legged Essay (a type of essay required in the imperial examination). The Eight-Legged Essay is a great essay discussing the Way of sages, and its subject matter is "cutting out several small pieces from the Confucian classics." Its thoughts cannot go beyond the classics, and are not the author's own. This is truly the act of "binding people's hearts and suppressing thoughts." The current writing of short essays is not necessarily the same. If one insists that the current short essay is equal to the Eight-Legged Essay, then that Eight-Legged Essay is definitely not the kind used for "testing scholars," but another kind. Behind the stone-printed "Romance of the Western Chamber" circulating in the market, there are often attached sixteen Eight-Legged Essays by Tang Yin, which take a line of lyrics from each act of "Romance of the Western Chamber" as the topic. This is somewhat similar to a certain type of short essay today, but is still much more constrained in form.

In ancient times, in addition to the Eight-Legged Essay, there was also the "Policy Question" (策問), also called "Responding to Policies" (對策), for "testing scholars." The questions and answers were about major political and economic issues, so they were also great essays. However, few of these great essays were good. Why? Without practical investigation and research, the basis for answering the policies was only a few Confucian classics, histories, philosophical works, and literary collections. Therefore, although the framework was large, the content was still empty.

Nothing can be generalized. It is good to do big topics, but it is not necessarily a waste of effort to do small topics. Mount Tai does not reject soil, and rivers and seas do not reject small streams. Small things may be helpful to big things, or at least they can coexist without hindrance. Most people in the world are limited by their talents and abilities, and some people can only do small businesses and small topics. If there are great talents who look down on these, they can go and do great undertakings and big topics themselves. At that time, with "big and small thriving," society will be much more lively and culture will progress faster.

Looking at China today, there is basically nothing. No matter what kind of undertaking, it will be criticized by grand discussions at the beginning and end in destruction, while those who make grand discussions do not do great undertakings themselves. This phenomenon is not good. I believe that the most important thing to do today is to "do one's best."

That buried volcano! It will always bring about your future collapse!

Melancholy Malaya, distant Selangor!

You make me disgusted, but you also make me nostalgic. There remains a beautiful child,

Her pure heart, waiting for my return,

But I am a white cloud in the sky, drifting aimlessly,

No one can predict when we will meet again?

× × ×

I drift towards the vast ocean; the southern breeze will blow away the foreign dust covering my face.

In the north, a red glow hangs in the sky,

There is the bright homeland cloud!

Although that is not necessarily the paradise I yearn for,

But there, the raging tide of truth is surging forward.

× × ×

Goddess left in the melancholy country!

I hope you stop your earnest prayers,

The dust of foreign lands has made me depressed,

I want to drift to the fanatical northern country!

"Weishui Xuan Diary" (Part 2)

— Shu

Four

In "Weishui Xuan Diary," there are three main travelogues that can be extracted: "A Journey to Qiyun Mountain," "A Journey to Baiyue Mountain," and "A Record of Wulin." These three records can represent the travelogues in the diary. Fragmentarily speaking, as "Record of Qiyun Mountain" says, "All day long walking between two mountains, one peak spitting clouds, one peak sending the sun, wild pine trees along the road, steamed by rain and baked by the sun, the fragrance assaulted the senses, and the sleeves were stained, and when twisted, they all had the aroma of dragon musk." As in "The weather is newly clear, and it feels even more clear and bright. The peaks have a clear morning color, dragging blue sunlight on them, the distant ones like vermilion flags in mid-air, the near ones like gilded and embroidered, with red maples and green cypresses dotted in between, ten thousand valleys storing clouds, and a thousand streams washing jade. At this point, I think that Li Zhaodao, the prince, did not set up all the rules for nothing. The size of the Mi school is like the Zhongshu Hall (Secretariat), with light ink as the judge's signature, and it is comprehensive." The description of the changing scenery is extremely vivid, and the writing is also very clear. "Record of Paying Homage to Baiyue Mountain" mostly records distances, personnel, meetings with friends, and visits to calligraphy and paintings, without special characteristics, except for "Hang Travel," which is short and eloquent. The book describes many times of traveling to Hangzhou, but only this trip is better. On the tenth day of the seventh month of Yimao, it says: "It was very hot. In the evening, Tan Mengxun prepared a small boat with wine and fruits to take me and my son for a cruise, starting from the lotus flower house, deep in the lotus leaves, going upstream to the inner six bridges, out to the three bridges, and arriving at the Lakeside Pavilion. We sat in a circle on the stone platform. At that time, the bright moon gradually appeared, and a refreshing breeze came suddenly, washing away the vexing heat. On the way back, we talked about poetry with great interest, pointing out the old residence of Sun Taichu, and sighing for it!" On the fifteenth day, it said, "Looking north from Su Causeway, the lights floating on the water are like gold, glittering and sparkling. The people of Hangzhou who are too poor to bury their dead throw their bones into the water of the Broken Bridge, and the custom of the Ghost Festival is such that the men and women of the city go boating on the lake at night, and all the boats, big and small, are rented out until dawn. However, only the northeast half is like boiling water. As for Hunan, there is a silent moonlit scene, illuminating a few groups of tap dancers. On the way back, we stayed for a while at Yuhuwawan. Mengxun pointed to a dilapidated house in the misty trees and said, 'This is where Tang Hanfu of Jinhua lived, closing the door all day to refine golden elixir. I don't know if he succeeded? We agreed to visit him in a while.'" The description of the scenery of the lake, the customs of the people, and the beauty of the night tour is no less touching than "Dreaming of Seeking." It is a pity that such descriptions are rarely seen in Li Rihua's diary.

Five

There is a special charm to Li Rihua's diary that I cannot help but mention again, and that is the part about writing about the weather, or the simple one or two lines of daily records, which are sometimes extremely inspiring. For example, writing about the sound of birds, "On the eighth day, it was sometimes rainy and sometimes sunny, and the weather was excellent, and the sound of birds was like the voice of Buddha." "Ninth day. In the dense green shade of the trees, there was a slight drizzle from time to time. The sunlight flashed through the clouds. I sat idly in the beautiful Yinyin Pavilion, listening to the sound of birds, which was extremely clear and pleasant." "Eighth day. The fine rain steamed and was humid, and the lacquered utensils were all sweating, and the sound of birds did not stop." What is recorded is only a dozen words, but a kind of leisurely life and poetic interest is revealed behind the paper. Also, as in, "Twenty-first day. The plum blossoms are already scattered, and shepherd's purse can be picked, and from now on, spring will be approaching day by day." "Third day. Cheng Kefan sent a blackbird as a gift, and the marriage family Zhang sent a pot of lilies, with thirty-six flowers budding and blooming, and from then on, I spent all day among the fragrance of flowers and the songs of birds." Both the artistic conception and the text can be deeply savored. However, no matter how much you try to escape the world, due to the connections of life, it is impossible in reality. Although Li Rihua did not worry about food, clothing, and housing, he was still inevitably filled with indignation about the world. When talking about people and affairs, he could not help but "sigh and lament." On another day, he said at length, "In recent days, I have been mediating disputes for people, and I feel that in this world, those who rely on their own opinions act arbitrarily, and those who are contrary to others will inevitably kick and bump. The waves are dangerous and terrifying. I now know that the ancients' retreat and concession are truly a cup of sweet dew in great vexation. Shen Zigang came and we drank wine while eating crab. Talking about this made it even more flavorful." This not only shows his indignation and why his life went into seclusion, but also can be inferred. (The End)

Leaping the Ladder (5)

— Cao Ming

At night, A-Han, half asleep, his body ruined by fatigue, pressed coarsely and heavily on the weak woman, and the woman cried out softly because she could not breathe comfortably:

"Be careful, I haven't had my period for three months, don't..."

"Really?" The man was filled with joy, and his body contracted because he was overly careful.

The sun was already leaning to the west, and the light shone from behind the small thatched hut beside the field, casting a gray, irregular square shadow in front of the door of the hut; an old woman and a young man with tanned skin were squatting in this shadow.

"It must be like this," the old woman said, rolling a paper cigarette with her head lowered, "I heard that Master Deng's father was also a poor bachelor, and when his mother was pregnant with him丨丨you know she was very pious哪丨丨she leaped the ladder on the nineteenth day of the ninth month, 'Guanyin's Birthday'……… You…

Look how wealthy and capable Master Deng is now!" The old woman stared at the rice fields with hopeful eyes.

"Leap the ladder, call our A-Mei leap the ladder? 丨丨" The man said hesitantly, smacking his lips.

"Forget it, forget it, sensible women often don't care about these things. Third Aunt and Fourth Niang both say that I have a good idea... We can't let poverty entangle our descendants. The next generation is important!" The old woman said forcefully and quickly. As a result, she went back with a triumphant smile.

On the nineteenth day of the sixth month, a solemn and expectant commotion arose outside A-Han's house. Two or three women dressed neatly, with slightly anxious faces, poked half their bodies in and asked carefully:

"Is everything all set up, Fourth Aunt?"

"Well, yes, you first move the fruit box and incense candles to the temple, A-Han..." the old woman said hurriedly, jumping like a grasshopper.

"Drink this sip of holy water," the mother-in-law held a bowl of clear water that had been left over from the "Seventh Sister Festival" last year, and said gently to her daughter-in-law, "After you drink it, I will go with you to worship Guanyin Niangniang, and leap the ladder in front of her altar, and you will definitely give birth to a blessed son..."

A-Mei followed her mother-in-law to the Guanyin Temple in a daze. The encouraging and respectful gazes of the people surrounding the temple door confused A-Mei. She mechanically listened to her mother-in-law's commands and knelt and worshiped without missing a beat.

In an open space in front of the altar of the Guanyin Temple, two square fir tables were placed, with a wooden ladder, the kind normally used to ascend to a god's altar, sandwiched in between. A bamboo ladder was then tied to it with straw rope, standing strangely and arrogantly in the joint of the two square tables, like a man-eating, long-legged demon. Many people held up the tables. A low wooden stool was also placed beside the square table.

A "god worshiper" prostrated herself on the open space and prayed, then stood up and walked devoutly to the pregnant woman standing there in a daze, saying:

"Sister-in-law Han, step on the low stool, climb onto the table on the right, and then climb up one step at a time, cross over the last step, and climb down from the left step by step," the old devotee continued with special effort, "Tell the Greatly Compassionate and Greatly Merciful, give birth to a wealthy and intelligent son, tell the Greatly Compassionate and Greatly Merciful!"

"Can I climb that high--" A-Mei asked vaguely in a long, trembling voice, but no one heard her.

The urging eyes and the hissing sound of encouragement, like dogs fighting, numbed A-Mei's terror. She nimbly jumped onto the stool, jumped onto the table, and climbed up the ladder one step at a time. A chaotic chorus of praise rose beneath her feet. When she reached the middle of the bamboo ladder, the ladder shook like a willow tree; she continued to climb up, and the people below shouted frantically: "Virtuous woman, capable woman! ... Hurry, there are only two steps left, turn your body over啊!"

The small exchange market is slightly weak, and bond prices fluctuate, with US bonds being the most resilient. (Wheat) The drought has not abated, and buyers are flocking in, so prices are soaring. Field losses are increasing daily. Yarn and Cotton Yarn Rise Sharply Again in the Afternoon

Long positions emerge suddenly: Futures reach 85 yuan

The yarn market was flat in the morning and rose sharply in the afternoon. Because rumors were rife in the market, saying that Japanese yarn was trending upward. In addition, there were rumors that 4,000 pieces of Zhong brand 20-count yarn were exported. With these two major reasons, people's minds suddenly turned tense and buying surged. At the same time, the factories also closed down their spot yarn and were unwilling to sell it easily. As a result, the situation rose. A new high of 185.3 yuan since the new year was found.

Golden Rooster rises again by 2.6 yuan

The opening of the tender yarn in the morning was bleak, and the market was still flat. After bidding for two or three rounds, a part was sold, and the situation stabilized. Each month rose slightly by 0.1-0.2 jiao. In the afternoon, there were many rumors in the market, which were all beneficial to the long positions. Buying surged, and each month rose by 2.3-0.4 jiao to 3 yuan. The total transaction statistics for the whole day were 61,150 bales. It was found that Tongfu sold 1,050 bales, Jifeng 1,300 bales, Dafeng 900 bales, Suilong 900 bales, Yichang 1,150 bales, Dachang 1,200 bales, and Yuanfeng 100 bales. Xincheng bought 1,050 bales, Taichang 1,650 bales, Dafu 1,000 bales, Tongji 1,350 bales, Huikang 1,350 bales, Yicheng 900 bales, Senkang 900 bales, Chungi 800 bales, and Jinchang 900 bales. Cotton Follows the Rise by About Half a Yuan

The cotton market started flat and then rose. With the soaring yarn market, people were excited, and the cotton market also rose accordingly. However, Japanese merchants took the opportunity to make profits and sell a lot. The general retail investors had strong ideas, so as soon as the market loosened, buyers flocked in. In short, the inventory is relatively thin, but the overseas cotton market is generally flat.

Zheng Standard Cotton is Driven High by Yarn in the Afternoon Market

The opening price of the standard cotton in the morning market was softened by foreign cotton, and there was no change in each month. In the afternoon, the price of each month rose by 0.3-0.4-0.6 jiao with the sharp rise in the yarn market. The total transaction statistics for the whole day were 140,600 dan. It was found that Tongji sold 3,500 dan, Gengfeng 6,000 dan, Changfeng 6,800 dan, Yuanxingchang 4,900 dan, Yuanda 2,100 dan, Yuanda 2,200 dan, Yongchang 5,400 dan, Hengde 1,700 dan, and Changhe 1,500 dan. Yarn Exchange Appraises Standard Yarn Grade

丨Higher Grade Price for October Period by One Grade丨

Huagao Yarn and Cloth Exchange held a cotton yarn appraisal and review meeting on May 29 for the delivery of the November period. As a result, the grade increase and decrease price was raised by one grade compared with the grade price of the October period. In addition to the increase of one yuan for Chongxin Factory's 20-count Dafa brand, Shenxin Factory No. 1, 3, 5, and 6's 20-count Zhong brand was reduced by one yuan. However, the grade price of 10-count coarse yarn was increased by one yuan to four yuan, and the grade of 16-count yarn was the same as last time, with no change at all.

Yarn Exchange Increases Special Certificate for Cotton Flowers in This Month

Chinese Yarn and Cloth Exchange will increase the special certificate cash for new transactions of standard cotton from June 1st for the June period by three yuan per dan, and one party will be charged for each deposit. Notice is posted.

Foreign Cotton Drops Across the Board

Yesterday, US cotton was weak at first due to bad news from Liverpool, then strong due to foreign merchants buying in, and finally soft again due to manufacturers selling futures. As a result, spot goods fell by five pounds per British weight, and futures fell by six to seven pounds per British weight. British cotton futures fell by one to three points. Indian cotton was strong at first due to Japanese merchants buying in, but then returned due to speculators selling out. As a result, Pingle fell by half a rupee, Aumla rose by one rupee, and Bairokhi fell by two and a half quarters. The original telegram record is on the left (telegram on the 31st):

Grain and Flour Futures Rise in Unison

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, the market for each month suddenly showed a sharp rise. The quotation of foreign wheat in Chicago and Canada rose by 1.56 yuan. Moreover, there were rumors in the market that Russia had a tendency to purchase grain from China. Therefore, after the opening price, the minds of the near and far terms were exceptionally excited. At the same time, it was heard that the foreign exchange of the yarn and cloth gang was shrinking frequently, so they also purchased in large quantities. This state is no different from being revealed by speculative frenzy, causing the opening market to the closing market to be in a step-by-step tension. It is the first lively since the fall in flour prices. By the time the market opened in the afternoon, people's minds were still good, even closer to the morning. However, the Tianjin gang sold a large number of returns, so in the exciting moment, it had fallen slightly. Later, off-site speculation absorbed one after another, and the market was held. As for the factories, most of them were watching and not coming out, so the future market is still difficult to grasp, because once the factories come out, the market will inevitably change. As a result, this month rose by four and a half quarters compared to the end of the previous month, June and July rose by five and a half quarters, August rose by five quarters, September rose by four quarters, October rose by four and two and a half hairs, and November has already been sold, initially at 2.09 yuan, and the closing price is also good at 2.50 quarters.

Foreign Wheat Drives Up Wheat Futures

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat futures market in the morning, each month showed an exceptionally exciting state. The quotation of foreign wheat rose by about 1.56 yuan, so the market was shocked. Although the quotation of foreign wheat has not been fully related to the current demand, the market took the opportunity to vent the depression of the past few months, so from July to September, from the opening to the closing in the afternoon, buying was strong, and the market rose step by step. However, the inland gangs believed that the new wheat harvest was approaching, and if the weather remained unchanged within a week, a full harvest would be undoubtedly possible, so the number of people engaged in selling was also huge. There are changes after this situation, and the ups and downs must be great. As a result, July rose by seven cents, August rose by six cents, September rose by one jiao and one hair, October rose by one jiao, and the spot wheat market was still stable. There was very little delivery, and the price was unchanged. The opening price of Guide wheat was three yuan, and the opening price of Yaowan wheat was 2.97 yuan, totaling 500 bags, which were handled by Fuxin.

Rice Market Steps Up by More Than One Quarter

Rice Association Founding Anniversary Today, Stop Pecking for One Day

(Hu South) A total of fourteen or five late rice boats and eight or nine thick japonica and various colors (totaling more than 3,000 shi) arrived, and the situation was very tight. As soon as the late rice from various gangs was sold by the North China, Tianjin, and Weihaiwei gangs, the sellers shouted high. Those who were pregnant with goods took the opportunity to get a kick, but the result was just a boom, and the situation was flat afterward. Although Qingjiao, Songsi, and Liantang goods totaled more than 2,000 bags, the market only continued to rise by more than one chi. As for the thick japonica from various gangs, at first it only relied on the store's stomach to move around, and did not see any beautiful colors. Later, the Nanyang gang took the initiative to purchase more than 600 bags of Sutong japonica, and the seller once lifted it up, and the market color also turned tighter. The price of goods such as the Chang gang's Nangang all rose by more than two chi. Du Yangjian followed suit by a few cents, and Yinbianyuan also had beautiful colors. Today, due to the anniversary of the founding of the Rice Association in Shanghai, the colleagues celebrated by expressing congratulations, so it was decided to temporarily stop pecking for one day.

(Hu North) More than 20 boats arrived from various places in Hexia. The way out for each type of goods in the market, white japonica high-end goods were flat, medium and second-rate slightly melted, white yuan selected high continued to melt, medium and second-rate stomach was stagnant, thin rice transactions were flat, sheep Du Xian zero dismantling was not bad, and the port passenger pointed slightly moved. The market shape of japonica yuan was tightly buckled by a few cents, thin rice was added by one chi, sheep tip was added by nearly a jiao, and Du Port passenger was steadily standing.

Passenger Xian and Passenger Yuan Increase Sharply Again

Yesterday, the market situation of Passenger Xian, the office stomach of the local passenger was active, especially the Fuzhou gang of Fujian Province was the most greedy. The Fuzhou gang had retreated and watched when the front rose sharply last month. Recently, the office stomach has gradually become prosperous. It has been more lively in the past three days. Yesterday, it went to each rice for more than 4,000 bags, mainly brown rice. The inland gang selected and handled rice, and went to 790 bags yesterday, which were from Hunan Shashi. This street also paid attention to brown rice, but the number of trips was not large. However, the arrival head has decreased in recent days, and the vendors are not as active as before. Once the local passenger is smoothly handled, the market will see an upward exhibition. Yesterday, the mechanized brown rice returned to good across the board. In addition to the higher meter, the big market goods rose by nearly a jiao. After the Passenger Yuan rose sharply to more, the market turned to a flat trend. However, in recent days, this street and the Beiyang inland Fuzhou have all inquired. Yesterday, 800 bags of newly arrived Xiang Yuan, 300 bags of Wu Yuan, and 400 bags of returned goods were opened. Most of them were handled by this street, and the market price has been 20 to 30% higher than the previous market. The price of Hunan mechanized yuan is 9.7 yuan, and the price of Wuhu mechanized yuan is 10 yuan.

Wenzhou New Beans and Rapeseeds Have Been Listed

Yesterday, new goods from Wenzhou were listed, including two batches of new broad beans shipped by the Haiyan wheel, totaling 132 bags. The quality of the goods was better than last year, with a status of more than 85%. The price was 3.5 yuan, and it was purchased by the Tianjin gang. Two batches of new rapeseeds also arrived, with good quality and a status of 90%, totaling 450 bags. The price was 4 taels, and 260 bags, the price was 3 taels and 9 qian, which were all the stomachs of foreign merchants. The soybean factory's stomach is quite healthy, so the upper and middle goods are very tight. Yesterday, the factory's transaction included more than 90 bags of Guide beans, 3,000 bags of Xuzhou beans, four cars of Weixikou beans, two cars of Yingzhou beans, and the remaining small number were used by this street.

Sugar Market Sees Rumors of Increased Donations in Chaoqing Production Area

Yesterday, the sugar market was slightly better due to the tightening of customs gold. The public association allocated 24 raw sugar white allocations at 20.65 yuan, up 5% from the previous day. This bank's goods were 20.75 yuan, transshipment goods were 6.75 yuan, and Dutch red and Taikoo sugar were unchanged. The price of No. 1 cotton white in this factory was still 19.12 yuan. According to news from the production area of Chaoqing, there were rumors of increased donations and the land price was tightened again, so the goods of this number in this area, when the current inventory is getting thinner, were unwilling to sell lightly, and the asking price increased again, especially the upper village. It was heard that hundreds of bags of white sliced sugar had been secretly opened, up 12%, and the quality of the goods was good, which was not surprising for the second village. Yesterday, the owner of Xinghua Chi asked for 13.2 yuan, but it had not been formed. 140 pieces of Shimen sliced green were continuously opened, and 10 yuan and half a piece. There were some transactions for Huizhou white, and the goods rose by 18 yuan at a higher price. The standard Wufu white ice was shipped by the Jiahe wheel to more than 200 boxes yesterday. All parties are in need, and the price is expected to stand firm.

Spring Cocoons in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Report Good Harvests

Gongbu Cocoon Bank's Collection is Not Prosperous The cocoon banks in the Gongchen Bridge area have been opened for several days. The new cocoons of the early and late gangs in the four villages of Hangxian County are gradually listed. The improved species have the most abundant harvest, and the cocoon body is also superior. However, the cocoon banks' opening price is not high. The highest price of Sima scales for improved species of superior cocoons is only 345 yuan, and the price of native cocoons is 223 yuan. Farmers' silkworms are not cheap, and they are all suffering losses. Therefore, the number of collections in each bank is insufficient.

Xucun Has Many Self-Reeled Native Silks Most of the farmers in the villages near Xucun lost a lot of early native silkworms this year. The categories were all supplemented with dragonfly silkworms and improved species. The hatching was later, the leaf consumption was more, and the leaf price was not cheap. The cost of silkworms was heavier. The new cocoons have been listed for many days, and the cocoon banks have suppressed the price and collected them. The market scale improved species cocoons are only 30 yuan, and the native cocoons are 18 yuan. Most farmers are losing money, and most of them reel native silks themselves and sell them at a price.

Yixing Cocoon Banks Opened One After Another Yixing's various cities and villages have achieved the best results in this year's improved species. The instructor's guidance is effective, with ten years of experience. There are more than 20 cocoon banks in the four villages that have opened, and most of them contract and solve for Wuxi silk merchants. The early silkworm cocoons have been listed. Due to the sluggish overseas silk market, the cocoon banks have pulled together and collected improved species cocoons for 25 yuan to 30 yuan, and native cocoons for 15 yuan to 18 yuan.

Tunxi Zhenmei Soars

Yesterday, there was a drastic change in the foreign merchant tea market in this port. The market price of Tunxi Gaozhuang wholesale Zhenmei green tea plummeted to 105 yuan. Compared with the opening period, the market price was 245 yuan lower. Suian Zhenmei fell to 945 yuan, also 67 yuan lower than before. The situation was quite unfavorable. However, the inventory of Tunxi and Suian Zhenmei in the market was only 12,000 boxes. Yesterday, the market was almost searched and bought by companies such as Mianlong, Xiehe, and Tianyu. In the future, new goods from Shexian and Wuyuan will arrive in Shanghai, and it will be difficult to reverse the decline. As for the black tea market, the low-class goods in Wenzhou and Koukou are still selling smoothly, and the selling price is firm. However, the trading of medium and high-class goods in Qimen and Fuliang has suddenly become slack in the market yesterday, and the market is afraid that it will be difficult to stand firm.

Hardware New Iron Wire Arrives Continuously

Due to the shortage of new iron wire, the standard is quite strong. Because the bottom goods of the customer gangs are weak, there are many people who want to buy them. It was found that hundreds of barrels of new goods have been loaded in the past two days. For example, Gonghexing and New Taikoo have spot goods delivered.
